Mussolini's Ambition Will Focus on Africa in the Future 25

Asia is Considered its Periphery

The League of Nations and Disarmament are Interdependent

Rome - Today is the opening of the second five-year congress of the Italian Fascist Party. At four o'clock in the morning, Roman bugles sounded, calling on party members to prepare to attend. Approximately seven thousand key Italian Fascist Party members gathered in the Grand Theater to welcome party leader Mussolini. Amidst thunderous applause, Mussolini stood up and delivered a speech, stating that opening up Africa would be the work of Italians in the future. He said that Italy does not have a problem of conquering land. Italy, the country of Fascism, should not allow countries that create this problem to block its spiritual and economic development.

Mussolini spoke about foreign policy, saying that Austria can rely on Italy to maintain its independence and assist in its economic reform. Italy and Yugoslavia can also improve their relations when the environment is appropriate. As for the unresolved issues between Italy and France, although there has not been any real progress toward a resolution, relations between the two countries are constantly improving. The reform of the League of Nations depends on the outcome of the disarmament conference. If this conference fails, then the League of Nations does not need to be reformed, because the failure of disarmament is enough to announce the end of the League of Nations. Countries that are armed cannot, of course, oppose the implementation of the equal rights granted to Germany in 1932.

Mussolini also said that Italy's disarmament memorandum is a very reasonable plan to promote understanding between large and small European countries. Without this understanding, Europe will be doomed and headed towards darkness. Mussolini continued by saying that it is important for Italy to find a way out in Africa and spoke of the possibility of cooperation with Asia, saying that Italy is only a few hours away from Africa and Asia by sea, and even less by plane. Mussolini said that the mission he entrusts to modern and future Italians should not be misunderstood. This is not a matter of land conquest, but of natural expansion to lead to the cooperation of Italy with the people of Africa and the East. It is also a matter of using the infinite resources of Africa and Asia to introduce civilization to the world. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Mussolini Reiterates His Proposal to Revise Treaties 26

Supplement to the Italy-Austria-Hungary Protocol

Hungary Confronts the Little Entente

Rome - In a speech this morning to prospective members of the Chamber of Deputies, Mussolini's section on Hungary is generally regarded as a supplement to the political protocol agreed upon by Italy, Austria, and Hungary yesterday. Because when the leaders of the three countries were negotiating in Rome, some major problems arose from the Hungarian side. At that time, Hungary argued that the protocol answered by Hungary should mention the revision of the peace treaty. Subsequently, the treaty terms did not mention the revision of the peace treaty. This is an omission method. It was agreed that the day after the treaty was signed, the Italian government would issue a declaration on this issue. The nature of Mussolini's speech this morning regarding Hungary is equivalent to this declaration. In this speech, the leader of the Italian government stated that he supported the return to Hungary of the territory of the Magyars (i.e., Hungarians) that was ceded to the Little Entente countries by the peace treaty. This is a kind of guarantee from Italy to Hungary. According to estimates in diplomatic circles, Mussolini has made many declarations regarding the revision of the peace treaty. This statement is only a restatement of previous declarations and does not imply that Italy, Austria, and Hungary are negotiating to confront the Little Entente. Not only do various newspaper commentaries and the preface to the political protocol recognize that the agreement signed yesterday is the starting point for broader negotiations, but Mussolini himself solemnly stated this point in his speech this morning. Hungary has always believed that it cannot cooperate with the Little Entente countries alone, and that even economic cooperation is impossible. The concern is that doing so would entail losing some of Hungary's independence, or at least its moral independence. Now that there is a tripartite agreement, if Hungary cooperates with the Little Entente, Austria and Italy will back it, and Hungary will no longer oppose cooperation. And judging from Mussolini's speech, Italy has already admitted its hope that Hungary will cooperate with the Little Entente countries. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Mussolini's Remarks Greatly Surprise the French 27

Believed to be Enough to Aggravate the Turbulent Situation

(Paris) - The French press expressed surprise at Mussolini's speech. While the French press does not object to the tripartite agreement, it believes that Italy's remarks regarding the Treaty of Versailles strongly advocate treaty revision, and that its hopes for an Italian-French understanding are in vain. Le Journal de Paris stated that Mussolini's speech seemed to want to impose his will on the world. Le Petit Parisien stated that Mussolini's remarks will create a turbulent atmosphere and feelings of disappointment. Le Figaro stated that France has tried to understand Italy's position, but Mussolini's remarks did not express any understanding towards France. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

(Paris) - News of the speech delivered last night by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini at the National Opera House to prospective members of the Chamber of Deputies has arrived here, and the entire French press regards it with great disappointment. Le Petit Parisien wrote, "Is it possible for the Italian Prime Minister to improve relations between Italy and Yugoslavia while describing the exploitation of isolated Hungary? The result will only make the Little Entente countries unhappy. At this time, Italy wants to spiritually improve the atmosphere and establish an understanding with the Little Entente countries, but how can it be content with the status quo and blame each other for accumulating problems that are difficult to reverse? Furthermore, the Italian Prime Minister's words, on the one hand, praised Italy's military strength while mentioning the disarmament conference, and his tone was extremely firm, as if giving orders. Its self-contradiction is self-evident. The declaration of this intention will only create an atmosphere of turbulence and a psychology of disappointment." Le Petit Journal expressed its opinion, saying that the Italian Prime Minister's intention to revise the peace treaty is obvious, which will hinder the progress of future negotiations. L'Écho de Paris expressed deeper disappointment, saying that Mussolini's remarks have never been so abrupt. He failed to adopt a peaceful attitude with a calm mind because he has proposed many initiatives in diplomacy over the past year, most of which have failed. This is why he encouraged the emotions of the audience with frantic words. The leftist newspaper Le Nouveau Siècle also held the same view, saying, "In the future, France should adopt only one attitude, that is, adhering to the consistent principle of security guarantees. What is the principle? That is, disarmament progress is impossible until security guarantees are obtained. As for the Four-Power Pact, it no longer exists. It has been sent to the grave by Mussolini. Mussolini concluded a political agreement with Austria and Hungary without first consulting the signatory countries of the pact." The socialist newspaper Le Populaire criticized, saying that Mussolini firmly ordered that the country should reach military strength and concentrate the lives of the entire country on military force. Mussolini's intention is to allow us to regard this as a lesser harm. What a strange mentality! (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers Explain the Rome Agreement 28

Reforming the Danube Economy

Neither Cooperation nor Struggle

Vienna - The Graz daily newspaper "Tagespost" interviewed Prime Minister Dollfuss and obtained his statement, which stated, "The purpose of the Rome talks between Italy, Austria, and Hungary is not to form a united front to engage in struggle. On the contrary, it is to solve the major economic problems in the Danube River basin and restore natural economic conditions under the current political system. The natural economic conditions were destroyed by the last World War. This is one of the main reasons for the economic panic in the Danube River basin. Therefore, our goal is cooperation, not struggle. I am convinced that the results of the Rome talks have brought us closer to this goal." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Budapest - Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös returned here from Rome at 10:30 this evening. During a radio broadcast speech, he briefly stated that when he took office as Prime Minister, he criticized the European Union plan proposed by the late French Foreign Minister Briand, believing that the plan was too ambitious and that there were many obstacles to its implementation. At that time, he advocated a simpler and easier-to-implement plan. The purpose of this trip to Rome was nothing more than to realize this concept. All agreements made in Rome are completely open, and all countries can join. The governments of Italy, Austria, and Hungary also tried to eliminate the tendency of economic isolationism during the Rome talks. Therefore, Hungary's political and economic status will be greatly enhanced as a result. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Vienna - Prime Minister Dollfuss of Austria has returned from Rome and has arrived here. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Belgium Expresses Security Guarantee Measures 30

First Improve the Rhine Pact

Then Conclude Another Military Agreement with France

Brussels - Senator Seghers, chairman of the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee, published an article in "Le XXe Siècle" entitled "Dealing with Germany," which describes what guarantees Belgium should increase in order to allow Germany to rearm. The guarantees he proposes include two types: one is the Rhine Security Pact, which Belgium requires to improve the Rhine Security Pact signed in Locarno, especially regarding the point of view of using the pact, which should be improved. The second is a military agreement. In order to implement the Rhine Security Pact, another military agreement should be concluded with France so that Belgium can concentrate its military forces to defend itself in the event of a sudden attack. If Belgium's own danger increases, then it should make every effort to ensure that Britain also signs a practical military agreement with Belgium to immediately provide military assistance if Belgium is invaded. Only in this way can Belgian territory no longer be

invaded by other countries. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

One Wave Has Not Yet Subsided and Another Has Arisen: Germany Demands the Navy Again 31

Only Four Battleships Currently

(Berlin) - Germany's navy has always been bound by the Treaty of Versailles, but the strength of the German navy is still less than the limit allowed by the Treaty of Versailles. According to the treaty, Germany can have eight battleships, but in reality, Germany only has four battleships serving in the country. Among those four battleships, three belonged to the former Imperial Navy. The other one is the famous pocket battleship "Deutschland." Its speed is 26 knots per hour, and it is equipped with 18 cannons. There are currently two similar pocket battleships under construction. Germany has four brand-new cruisers in service, each displacing 6,000 tons, and three old cruisers as reserves. Among the reserve ships, there is also an "Emden" displacing 5,400 tons, which is currently being repaired in the dock. According to the provisions of the treaty, Germany can have eight cruisers. Germany currently has twelve torpedo boats in service, each displacing 800 tons, and four old torpedo boats are in reserve. The maximum limit stipulated by the treaty is 24 torpedo boats. However, Germany has no submarines or aircraft carriers because it is restricted by the treaty. In addition to the above-mentioned fleet, the rest of the German naval ships are insignificant. The Treaty of Versailles limits the German naval military strength to 15,000 tons. Germany's attitude towards maritime armaments is the same as that of land armaments. Germany has expressed dissatisfaction with its own disarmament, so it insists on the reduction of armaments by other countries. Germany's foreign policy is to demand equal rights and stop all countries from discriminating against Germany. Therefore, if all countries have submarines and aircraft carriers, then Germany should also have these rights, because this matter is related to Germany's national system and security. On the other hand, even if Germany adopts a plan to revitalize the navy, there is no hope of implementing and competing with other countries in naval shipbuilding. (National Telegraph on the 19th)

The Baltic States Alliance is Difficult to Achieve Temporarily 32

Latvia Continues to Work Hard

Therefore, Latvia continues to work hard to promote the alliance of the Baltic States, which is necessary. However, after fifteen years of efforts, the alliance of the Baltic States has not been realized, so it cannot be hoped that it will be realized once and for all in a short period of time. (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

Case of the Assassination of the Former Prime Minister of Romania 34

The Murderer is Being Tried by a Military Tribunal

Bucharest - Three members of the dissolved Iron Guard and fifty accomplices are accused of assassinating Prime Minister Duca on December 30. The trial opened today by a military court. The authorities decided not to hold a public trial, and even reporters were not allowed to attend, but the court can issue a communiqué for public knowledge. It is reported that the accomplices include people from all social classes, from nobles to others. The defendants have hired fifty lawyers, and four hundred people have been summoned to testify. This is truly one of the most shocking cases in Europe after the war. It was found that former Prime Minister Duca was assassinated at the Sinaia station on December 30 after meeting with King Carol, and died on the spot. One of the assassins fired three shots in a row at Duca's head and threw a bomb, and was immediately arrested by the police. His name is Constantin Nasa, a student. Two other accomplices were also arrested at the station at the same time. They are all members of the Iron Guard who oppose Jews. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

Interference in Politics by the Japanese Military 35

Minister of the Army Hayashi Establishes an Investigation Agency

Must Ask About Domestic Affairs and Diplomacy

(Tokyo) - Based on the intentions of Minister of the Army Hayashi, the army will establish a large investigation agency to deliberate on national policy after the parliament is closed. After the investigation results are determined, the military authorities' requirements will be submitted to the government. Minister of the Army Hayashi has generally followed the policies of his predecessors, but the army's views on the internal affairs conference are only abstract and conceptual, without proposing any specific cases. Although Minister of the Army has views about the current domestic and international situation and is not contradictory to those of former Minister of the Army Araki, if he only vaguely discusses without proposing a concrete case as the representative of the army, it will only make the situation more confusing. Therefore, he decided to speak from this perspective, carrying an irrefutable case, presenting it to the government, and gradually urging the government to research and implement it. This is the conclusion that Minister of the Army has recently reached. As for the name of the investigation committee, it is probably the Military and Political Investigation Committee, which is actually presided over by Chief of the Military Affairs Bureau, Major General Tetsuzan Nagata. The investigation items not only include domestic issues, but also external issues. All agencies will mobilize and turn the results of the investigation into conclusions. Therefore, it will take considerable time for the investigation committee to produce a conclusion. Minister of the Army Hayashi has personally come forward to deliberate on national policy, and it is expected that its impact will be great, so all parties attach great importance to it. (Telegraph dispatch on the 19th)

American Sends Currency Expert to China to Investigate the Silver Situation 36

Roosevelt's Advisor Rogers to Depart Soon

To Study the Economy in China, Not Responsible for Negotiations

(Washington) With President Roosevelt's approval, the Department of Treasury is now sending currency expert Professor Rogers to China

to investigate the silver situation. Professor Rogers is President Roosevelt's trusted advisor and a proponent of currency control policies. He will depart soon. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated today that Professor Rogers' trip to China does not imply any qualification for official negotiations; he will only focus on studying the economy. As soon as Rogers' mission to China was announced, the silver proposals of Representatives Dyer and others, which had been opposed by the Department of Treasury, were introduced in the House. Speaker of the House Rainey expects the bill to pass with a majority, but some believe that this bill will cause a violent conflict. (Reuter's, 19th)

American Labor-Management Conflict 37

A Major Problem in the Recovery Process

The Government Faces a Dilemma

(Washington) The beginning of this week is filled with labor-management conflict crisis. Although Congress has many important bills this week, they all seem insignificant compared to the brewing labor unrest. The automobile industry is at the forefront of commercial recovery, and the railway industry is the lifeline of national transportation, and there are rumors of labor unrest in both. Yesterday, one million railway workers, represented by 21 labor unions, rejected the proposal of the Railway Bureau Committee to continue reducing wages by one-eleventh for another ten months after the end of June. At the same time, American Federation of Labor President Green claimed that if automobile factories still do not recognize the union, 100,000 automobile factory workers will strike on March 21. National Recovery Administration General Johnson is scheduled to go to New York tomorrow to attend the labor-management conference in the automobile industry, hoping to find a way to prevent the strike from happening. The attitude of the railway union is also particularly worrying. A few weeks ago, President Roosevelt said that wages would still be paid according to the current regulations, but the union replied that railway workers have sacrificed a lot, while railway shareholders have benefited a lot during this recovery period, so they will not agree to extend the wage reduction plan for another ten months. What the railway industry is fighting for is wages, while the focus of the automobile industry dispute is the union. According to Article 7 of the Recovery Administration's automobile industry regulations, workers have the right to organize unions without interference, restraint, or threat from employers. Now automobile owners are organizing company unions, which obviously violates this provision, so the owners' position is vulnerable to attack on this point. If the authorities amend this provision, workers who have already joined the union can be exempted from the obligation to pay union fees, which is unacceptable to the leaders of the AFL. Furthermore, if the owners can maintain their company unions, the power of the AFL will be reduced, and its opportunity to expand will also decrease. However, if the owners are stubborn and the government has to declare company unions illegal, then employers' threats to labor will inevitably occur, causing endless disputes. American labor has only had a partial connection with extreme political ideologies in its history, which is different from other industrialized countries. However, if the United States enters a stage of severe labor-management conflict, this situation will not be maintained for long. Therefore, although Congress has the Philippine Independence Act, the Cotton Tax Act, the Securities Exchange Management Act, and the Naval Appropriation Act, which are all important events that need to be dealt with urgently, their importance pales in comparison to the impending labor unrest. (Reuter's, 19th)

Four Major American Bills 38

Listed on the Congressional Agenda for Voting Today

(Washington) The U.S. Congress has placed the four most recent major bills on the agenda. These four bills have been studied by hundreds of experts, and once voted on, the direction Congress will take in the future will be clearly indicated. The four major bills are as follows: (1) The Bankhead Cotton Restriction Act, which proposes to impose a restriction tax on cotton production exceeding 10,000,000 bales. (2) The Philippine Independence Act, which is a revision of the previous Philippine Independence Act (agreed upon by Senator Quezon, Chairman of the Philippine Independence Movement Committee, President Roosevelt, and congressional leaders). (3) The Fessinger Silver Purchase Act, which authorizes the Department of Treasury to purchase silver as a currency reserve and to issue silver securities that can be exchanged for silver bars equal to the price of gold. (4) The Thomas Silver Act, which authorizes the government to pay for foreign purchases of American surplus agricultural products with silver at a price higher than the world market price. According to Bankhead and Jones, chairman of the Agriculture Committee, today, the Bankhead Cotton Restriction Act can be passed safely tomorrow. However, observers predict that the number of votes for and against the bill will be very close, because Republican congressmen strongly oppose the bill, calling it "authoritarian" and "un-American," because some Democratic congressmen also sympathize with the Republicans' actions, as they are quite opposed to mandatory production cuts. The government hopes that the Philippine Independence Act can be passed in both the Senate and the House of Representatives tomorrow. The bill will be discussed before the silver bills and should not cause any problems. The bill will extend the previous Philippine Independence Act, which expired on January 17, to October 17, and also proposes to withdraw American land and naval bases in the Philippines in ten years. The outcome of the vote on the two silver bills tomorrow may be problematic, as President Roosevelt conducted eleven hours of secret research beforehand and his attitude is unknown. However, observers believe that the Thomas bill has a better chance of passing, because Fess's silver bill contains amendments to the government's current monetary plan. According to Thomas himself, in a conversation with an Associated Press reporter, he is confident that his proposed silver bill can be passed. (National Telegram, 18th)

Seattle Chemical Industrial Plant to Move to Shanghai 39

Seattle According to today's news, the Seattle Pacific Ammonia Company's chemical industrial plant will soon be moved to Shanghai. The plant was recently sold by Hengxin Gunpowder Company, and the buyer's name is unknown. Company officials declined to comment on the sale of the plant, saying only that it was unrelated to Spalding's trip to Shanghai. It is learned that Spalding's mission to Shanghai may be to build a first-class acid chemical plant in Shanghai. The plant is currently being dismantled, and all machinery and supplies will be shipped to Shanghai in about two weeks. (National Telegram, 18th)

The convening of these talks was originally the fervent hope of cotton industry colleagues. U.S. Navy Forms Expeditionary Force to Deploy Along Alaskan Coast 41

Scheduled to Depart from Seattle on May 1st

Preparing for Action After the Expiration of Naval Treaties

(Tokyo) According to a recent report from Consul Uchiyama in Seattle to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the U.S. Navy's 13th Naval District authorities are organizing an expeditionary force consisting of six large aircraft and six mine-laying ships to conduct research on ocean meteorology and flight range along the Alaskan coast. The ships are scheduled to depart from Seattle on May 1. Chairman Chiang Explains the Significance of the New Life Movement 42

To Make Life Simple and Orderly

Hoping for United Efforts to Promote It

(Nanchang) On the morning of the 19th, the Garrison Headquarters held a memorial week. Provincial education directors, secretaries-general, administrative commissioners, and generals who came to Jiangxi for training all participated. Led by Chairman Chiang, after performing the ceremony, he explained the significance of the New Life Movement, saying that the general life of Chinese people can be summed up as romantic, decadent, lazy, and dirty. The New Life Movement is not a new invention, but inherits the virtues of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame left by our ancestors, to make a modern person a good citizen. The so-called militarization of life is not a special thing, but to make life simple, orderly, uniform, disciplined, time-saving, and practical. This is the purpose of the New Life Movement. Last night, I saw the lantern parade. No matter who, whether in coarse clothes or fine clothes, the buttons were all buttoned up. This is the result of the New Life Movement since its launch. Buttoning buttons is a small thing that everyone can do. If all the people in the country are like this, it will shock foreigners. Therefore, to promote something, start with small, easy, and shallow things. Once guided, it can be done naturally without compulsion. I hope that all provincial civil and military officials, in governing politics, military affairs, education, and civil affairs, will act accordingly. (Central News Agency, 19th)

We should expand and enlarge the spirit and habits of the Dawn Movement to promote the New Life Movement with a good foundation. It is easier to achieve results than in other provinces. Our country has many open ports and many coastlines. However, blocking tools, such as torpedo boats and cruisers, are also easier to do in terms of financial resources. Central and National Government Memorial Weeks Reports 50

Zhu Jiahua: New Life and Education

Ju Zheng: Use Heavy Penalties in Times of Disorder, and Give the Benefit of the Doubt to the Innocent

(Nanjing) The Central Government held Premier Sun Yat-sen's Memorial Week at 9:00 AM on the morning of the 19th. Central Committee member Ye Chucang and more than a thousand staff members attended. Zhu Jiahua chaired the meeting and reported on the relationship between the New Life Movement, saying that the New Life Movement is a national revival movement that emphasizes propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Everyone should start with themselves and expand it, and pay attention to the new life of the general public in society. However, the issue of education is closely related to this movement. Mr. Chiang saw the danger of the nation and the country and paid special attention to moral cultivation, emphasizing propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. However, the new life of the general public in society is often contrary to this. Many people are romantic, undisciplined, and irresponsible. Officials are corrupt, and students are making troubles. This is all due to the lack of purpose and methods in past education. The Central Committee meetings decided to pay special attention to the determination of the purpose of education, and to revive the nation as the consistent purpose of education. After the September 18th Incident, we paid more attention to the implementation and methods of the purpose of education. At that time, we had rectified the academic atmosphere, rectified the university associations, reorganized the academic system at all levels, and prescribed the curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools to cultivate a good academic atmosphere with ancient history, love of the country, and love of the nation, and to promote compulsory education, save education funds, cultivate education talents, and increase the opportunity for students to study. Although the government has these regulations, it cannot be promoted due to the deep-rooted bad habits in society. It often feels difficult when promoting policies. The New Life Movement is to promote the habit of cultivating a new life for students through great social strength in the efforts of education. (Central News Agency, 19th)

(Nanjing) The National Government held a memorial week on the morning of the 19th. Ju Zheng, Chen Shuren, Cao Haosen, Deng Jiayan, Chen Qicai, Li Yuanding, Lu Chao, Wei Huai, and more than 300 staff members from various ministries, committees, and departments attended. Chairman Lin led the ceremony, and Ju Zheng reported on the topic of "Use Heavy Penalties in Times of Disorder, and Give the Benefit of the Doubt to the Innocent," meaning that our country is now moving towards the rule of law, and compared with advanced countries, there is only a difference in human customs. However, in recent years, due to political influence, social unrest, rural bankruptcy, and people forced by hunger and cold, many have fallen into the clutches of the law. The government has had to adopt a system of heavy penalties in times of disorder. If the law enforcers are not qualified and abuse penalties, the consequences will greatly affect the safety of the country and the rise and fall of the nation. Law enforcers should respect the role of criminal law on the one hand, and still understand the reasons for the crimes and always think of giving the benefit of the doubt to the innocent, so that those who are less guilty will not be wrongly sentenced. (Central News Agency, 19th)

National Conference to Promote Shipping Industry Holds Opening Ceremony This Morning 51

Ministry of Transportation Proposes Four Proposals

(Nanjing) The National Conference to Promote the Shipping Industry, convened by the Ministry of Transportation, is scheduled to open at the Ministry of Transportation Auditorium on the morning of the 20th. The opening ceremony will be held in the morning, chaired by Zhu, Ren of the Ministry of Transportation, who will report on the significance of the conference and invite President Wang to give a speech. If there is enough time in the morning, the first general meeting will be held, and the meeting will continue in the afternoon. The closing ceremony will be held on the afternoon of the 22nd, followed by a maritime administration meeting. By the evening of the 19th, nearly 100 proposals had been received. The Ministry of Transportation has drafted four proposals: (1) On the establishment of shipping policy, including the development plans of state-run and private shipping industries, with state-run developing ocean shipping and private developing inland river shipping. (2) On the development of the shipping industry, including advocating the concentration of financial resources, improving business operations, implementing integrated water and land transportation, and encouraging investment in emerging shipping industries. (3) Relations with international organizations (omitted). (4) Reducing shipping taxes and protecting shipping safety. (Special Dispatch, 19th)

(Nanjing) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company proposed to the shipping conference: (1) Establish a shipping control agency, whose main points advocate that whether it is a state-run or private agency, it should be subject to the control of the agency in business to achieve the effect of liaison and cooperation. Its content includes route distribution, combined transportation of goods distribution, commercial transport distribution, mail distribution, and the joint organization of transport companies. It is hoped that the business can develop into a business of 10 million, and the government will provide strong subsidies. (2) Reduce and exempt taxes on ship materials to reduce the burden. Li Yunliang, He Molin, and other representatives have brought them to Beijing to present to the conference. (Special Dispatch, 19th)

Government Establishes Pilotage Management Committee 52

(Nanjing) Because the pilotage rights are controlled by foreigners, which is related to national defense and the shipping industry, the government recently established a Pilotage Management Committee. The members are Total Customs Commissioner Meier He, Maritime Survey and Engineering Director Xi Liman, Staff Headquarters Lin Qi, Navy Department Xu Jixiang, Ministry of Transportation Gao Tingzi, and Shanghai Chamber of Commerce representative Chen Tianming, etc. It is planned to transfer the Chinese and foreign pilotage affairs in China to the committee for reorganization, guidance, and supervision. However, the water trade association of commercial groups from various countries in Shanghai refused to send representatives to participate in this meeting. Since its establishment, the association has held three meetings to discuss the first step to recover the Jiangjiang Company and the Japanese Kanlun organized pilot association organized by foreigners. However, the Jiangjiang Company has a total capital of 2 million yuan, so the results of the discussion still need to prepare funds to implement the recovery. According to the pilot staff of the Jiangjiang Company, there are a total of 32 people, and those who join the service must have more than ten years of captain qualifications, and must pass a strict examination and join the share capital of 50,000 yuan before they can serve. Therefore, British and Japanese people account for two-thirds, and only two Chinese people serve in the company, namely Sha Jiangjia and Lin Guojie. There are four pilotage sections, including Wusong, Hankou, Yichang, and Chongqing. (Special Dispatch, 19th)

International Commercial Telegram 57

—Special Commercial News Report from Reuters, March 19th—

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today (March 19th), the London gold price remains at 136 shillings and 6 pence, the same as Saturday's price.

London Silver: Today (March 19th), the London silver price for spot is 19 pence 875, and futures are 19 pence 9375, both down by 375. American and Chinese sellers were present in the morning, while buyers remained hesitant. Chinese buyers entered when the price fell, and the market stabilized at closing.

New York Silver Price: Today (March 19th), the silver market opened weaker due to news from London. Speculators adopted a wait-and-see attitude, awaiting news of the silver proposal, causing the market to loosen. Subsequently, sympathizing with other markets, the market showed a bearish trend. Opening futures prices fell by 40 to 67 points compared to Saturday's closing.

Bombay Silver: Today (March 19th), the Bombay silver market was quiet and without transactions.

Exchange Rates

Anglo-American Exchange Rate: Today (March 19th), the London foreign exchange market remains very quiet. The Anglo-American exchange opened at $5.09, the same as Saturday's closing price for the American-British exchange rate, then fell by 0.0625, but soon rebounded. The final price was $5.091875. Also, one US dollar equals 3 shillings and 11 and 1/34 pence in British currency.

Anglo-French Exchange Rate: Opened today at 77 francs 40, the same as the previous price. It fell by ten points in the morning, but then quickly rebounded, remaining at 77 francs 40.

New York Cotton: Today (March 19th), the cotton market opened weakly due to a slight resolution as the Penhead proposal had no action. Sellers increased as the South, local and foreign markets all sold, causing the market to loosen and prices to shrink.

Bombay Cotton: Today (March 19th), the Bombay cotton market was slightly loose due to some swap trading. The price for white cotton for April-May delivery was 202 rupees, down half a rupee from Saturday's closing.

Liverpool Cotton: Today (March 19th), the Liverpool cotton market was looser than before. At 1 PM, May futures were at 6.24, down three points.

Liverpool Wheat: Today (March 19th), the May futures price remained unchanged at 4 shillings and 3 and 1/25 pence.

Rubber

London: Today, the rubber market was relatively weak, as unsatisfactory sentiment was aroused by the prospect of restrictions. The trading price for April-June delivery was 4 pence and 31/32, down 1/875 from Saturday's closing. New York: Today (March 19th), the rubber market remained active, but also weakened due to the conditions in London and the lack of restriction news. However, buying interest was still strong when prices fell.

The Murder Portion of the Jin Shuren Case Has Been Adjudicated 67

Jin confessed to the course of the Hami Incident, saying that Hami was designated as a fiefdom during the Kangxi period, with a range of 300 li. Later, the presiding judge interrogated the course of the Xinjiang Incident in great detail, and presented accusations from various parties, including the Xinjiang Provincial Party Committee member You Qiwu, the Hui representative Mai Mai Di, and telegrams from Chu Minyi to Jin, telegrams from Mou Weitong to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, accusations from Ding Zhengxi and Yuan Jingyao and other fellow villagers from Gansu, and telegrams from Liu Wenlong, Sheng Shicai, and Hu Binglian and others from the Xinjiang Joint Association. Jin denied all of these one by one. At 4:00 PM, Aisha was interrogated, recounting Jin's crimes in Xinjiang and refuting Jin's confessions, saying that it was impossible for Ma Zhongying to instigate the local people. The cause of the incident was that Jin's troops forcibly married local women and seized land from the people. After the outbreak of the incident, the local people sued for peace, but Jin refused, leading to a situation that was out of control. The trial was completed at 5:10 PM, and it was decided to continue the trial of the portion of forcibly occupying the people's cultivated land on the afternoon of the 20th. After the trial, it will be temporarily suspended, and after further investigation of the evidence, the debate will begin. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

A Private Conference on British-Japanese Trade (London Correspondence) 92

British and Japanese Commercial Views Differ

Focus of Competition is on the Market

Both Export Cotton Yarn and Cotton Cloth

Conflict is to Seize Actual Benefits

Britain was originally a country that relied on interest income and occupied a dominant position in finance. Therefore, despite the fact that Britain's visible trade imports exceeded exports year after year, and despite the fact that its industrial organization was not as novel as Germany's or as acute as America's, it could still maintain its old style and gentlemanly attitude because its overseas investments were enough to control its national destiny and could control the world economy. However, since the European War, America has not only caught up with her, but also has a tendency to surpass her. Especially after the global economic panic occurred in 1939, most debtor countries gradually lost their creditworthiness. European countries such as Germany and Austria were almost bankrupt. South American countries such as Brazil and Argentina had to postpone the repayment of foreign investment interest, and new investments were naturally impossible to make. Moreover, the colonies and dominions were all caught in the global economic panic, and they had a tendency to seek their own liberation. Therefore, Britain's invisible trade imports declined very sharply. This had a great impact on the British national economy.

Britain, which previously did not rely much on the export of manufactured goods to fill the balance of international payments, now also painfully felt the necessity. Moreover, she still needs to import food and raw materials, which are indispensable for daily life and industrial operations. If Britain does not pay attention to the export problem, the future of the national economy will be somewhat dangerous. Therefore, since the Ottawa Imperial Economic Conference of the year before last, an economic alliance within the British Empire has gradually formed, with extremely strong protectionist trade colors. This action is of course important to the general economic relations of the world, but its impact on Japan is particularly serious, because although Britain is known as an industrially advanced country, the status of its heavy industry is not as important as that of cotton cloth. Japan, this newly emerging industrial country, also takes cotton yarn and cotton cloth as its second largest export. Not only has it become the hegemon of the west coast of the Pacific in the Far East market, but also British-controlled markets such as British India, Malaya, and Egypt have been invaded by Japanese cotton products and rayon products. Not only are they invading, but they are also surpassing Britain. Britain's textile products are in danger of being driven out by Japanese products. Therefore, last year's Indo-Japanese conference did not conclude until the end of the year.

However, the factors of struggle between Britain and Japan have not been eliminated, and there is still a tendency to continue to deteriorate. If it is really allowed to brew naturally like this, then the British measures to boycott Japan that were issued last year in India, Egypt, South Africa, Malaya, Australia, and other places will become even more severe, and the British-Japanese relations will further deteriorate. However, we know that Britain is good at observing the international situation and using diplomatic means to consolidate its own interests. She knows that it is not necessary to break with Japan at this time, and there is no need to break with Japan, so she still adopts her diplomatic methods to consult with Japan.

It is more appropriate to first have a meeting of representatives from the private textile industry to discuss more concrete solutions. Therefore, the representatives of the British and Japanese private trade conference held their first meeting at the British Board of Trade on February 14. The British representatives were Barrow, Mills, Gray, Cleria, Reese, and Tomson, five people. The representatives of the rayon industry were William and Spielman, two people. In addition, there was also the economic consultant Hughes, the secretary Street, Enzler, and the Board of Trade sent the Director-General of Commerce Lansiman and the Director of Overseas Trade Colville to attend. There were a total of twelve people attending from the British side. The Japanese representatives were Okada, Miyake, Mimura, Kawaguchi, and Tamagaki, five people from the cotton industry, and Shimada from the rayon industry, a total of six people attending.

Of course, it is difficult to predict what the outcome of the future meetings will be, but both sides have their own prejudices. On the British side: (1) The export of cotton cloth and rayon products should be based on the levels before 1931; (2) The agreement on exports to the market should focus on the proportion of exports in the whole world; (3) The sharp increase in the export of Japanese textile products in recent years should take into account the world situation and be slightly restricted. On the Japanese side: (1) The agreed export quantity should be based on 1933; (2) Britain itself and the British dominions and colonies should negotiate separately outside the market agreement; (3) The markets of third countries other than Britain and Japan must also be negotiated outside the agreement.

It is easy to imagine whether such a situation of each holding their own opinions can proceed smoothly. (February 12, 1934)

Japanese Troops Plan to Establish a Command Headquarters in Dolon 93

And actively building roads in eastern Chahar

Song Zheyuan Comes to Beiping to Discuss Defense Matters

Beiping Correspondence: Military Affairs Committee member Xiao Zhenying, upon receiving an invitation from Song Zheyuan to meet in Beiping, arrived in Beiping at 3:30 PM on the 16th via the Ping绥 Railway from Zhangjiakou. According to Xiao's account of the situation in eastern Chahar, "The Japanese army in Dolon recently announced a rotation of the 7th and 8th Divisions, and a portion of the Japanese army, under the pretext of increasing the number of districts in Guyuan (沽源) and Chicheng (赤城), has not yet withdrawn. They are also actively building roads, and Japanese aircraft in Dolon are conducting reconnaissance flights daily, transporting ammunition and supplies, engaging in very active military preparations. Therefore, a concrete plan must be devised regarding the defense of eastern Chahar. Some time ago, two company commanders from a certain regiment under Zhang Renjie's (張人傑) temporarily organized 2nd Division in the Guyuan and Chicheng area plotted wrongdoing, but were discovered by the regiment commander and placed under custody. That unit has been transferred to Zhangbei (張北) for reorganization, beginning the relocation on the 16th. The defense of the Guyuan and Chicheng area will be taken over by Zhang Zizhong's (張自忠) 38th Division. Zhang Renjie is currently still in Zhangjiakou. The Righteous Army's Battle in Sanxing 94

The National Spirit Does Not Die

The Struggle is Exceptionally Fierce

Colonel Iizuka Dies in Battle

Two Hundred Japanese Soldiers Annihilated

The puppet regime receives orders to take the stage. Under the heavy oppression, the people of the Northeast dare not speak out, swallowing their tears. The masses lack strong organization and are in the midst of a transition from agriculture to industry. Those with the strength and determination to resist are ultimately a minority. Among these minorities, some inevitably indulge in the volunteer army movement of national struggle for their personal gain. As a result, irregular behavior has occurred, arousing the resentment of the general public, and some have even become indignant and joined the enemy. Now that the enemy's foundation has gradually stabilized, the lies previously told are being broken one by one. The so-called "Kingly Way Paradise" has truly become a "Deadly Way Black Land." Some of the people of the Northeast naturally still cling to the present, guarding their meager properties, hoping to eke out a living. However, it is gradually becoming impossible to survive. The burden of taxes is almost twice as heavy as before, and agricultural products still cannot be sold. For example, a tax of one yuan must be paid annually for every ten chickens raised. Opium smokers trade everywhere, and the people's lifeblood is invisibly drawn away. Therefore, those who resist are becoming more determined, and the power of struggle is becoming stronger.

The Songhua River valley is the most fertile part of the undeveloped virgin land in the Northeast. The area has convenient water transport, with boats in summer and "Bali" (sledges) in winter. Now, automobiles are also operating. The cultivation of rice paddies is no less than that in the rice-producing areas of the South, and after years of hard work by our fellow countrymen, almost all of it has been developed. Since the Japanese invaded the Northeast, the first stage was focused on seizing political power and expanding their military deployment. The second stage was to use their massive military force to suppress the armed resistance movement of the Northeastern people, while at the same time directing the puppet regime to take the stage. Their major difficulty is the inability to realize their immigration plan, because the people of the Northeast eat sorghum rice, while the Japanese must eat white rice, and there are very few places in the Northeast that produce rice. Therefore, after much consideration and selection, the Japanese found Jiamusi, east of Sanxing, as their immigration area in northern Manchuria. There, water can be used for irrigation, and modern transportation is available for their use. As a result, the Japanese had three immigrations before this year, all of whom were prepared with full arms. In total, there were about 1,400 to 1,500 people, but 300 to 400 of them could not adapt to the northern climate and fled back. When these people arrived in Jiamusi, they began to enclose land. Chinese and Koreans within their areas were ordered to move away. Some were given meager compensation, while others had to swallow their tears and avoid them. As a result, the general public in the area harbors deep resentment towards the Japanese.

The Righteous Army was originally in a latent stage, but was forced to take action by the current situation. Therefore, a small group gathered east of Sanxing, planning to attack Sanxing on one side and Jiamusi on the other, hoping to obtain some weapons and equipment and then enter Hulin to live in the mountains, taking the opportunity to fight the Japanese again. Unexpectedly, Iizuka Tomoyoshi (飯塚朝吉), the commander of the 63rd Infantry Regiment of the 33rd Brigade of the 10th Division stationed in Sanxing, detected this. He dispatched a battalion of puppet troops, flanking left and right. Iizuka himself led a company of Japanese troops, heading down the central road, to attack Shilong Mountain—the gathering place of the Righteous Army—preparing to launch an attack from there on Sanxing, the base of the Righteous Army. The Righteous Army had just finished preparing, planning to depart on the afternoon of March 10 and launch a dawn attack on the 11th. Unexpectedly, the Japanese army arrived early on the morning of the 10th, just as the Righteous Army was fully prepared, launching a surprise attack. The puppet troops were only fighting as a formality. The Japanese encountered this tough opponent, and after three hours of fierce fighting, an entire company of Japanese troops was annihilated. Colonel Iizuka Tomoyoshi was killed, and company commander Suzuki Minoru (鈴木實) naturally could not survive either. Almost none of the remaining Japanese soldiers escaped with their lives. The Righteous Army's responding force was indeed small, but the fighting was very fierce, and the victory was rare since the beginning of the war of resistance. (March 12, Harbin)

Japanese Forcefully Seize Gold Mines in Xinglong County 96

The gold mine and river area covers more than 300 hectares

The original mine owner urges the Foreign Ministry to protest to the Japanese side

Tianjin Correspondence: Since last year, the counties near the Great Wall have been under Japanese pressure, and our political power has lost its operational efficiency. Among them, Xinglong County, most of which is outside the Great Wall, and Malanyu, where the Qing Tombs are located, are where most of the puppet Jehol army is stationed. A large Japanese army unit is also stationed there, and everything is subject to Japanese interference. The county magistrate has no power to implement policies or issue orders. Now, the county government has withdrawn from outside the Great Wall to Malanyu, effectively abandoning four-fifths of the county's land outside the Great Wall to the puppet state. This matter concerns the entire North China issue, so we cannot simply blame the county magistrate for incompetence. It is regrettable that the county is the most abundant gold-producing area in Hebei Province, and more than 20 gold mine licenses have been issued by the Hebei Industry Department over the years. Among them, the area of the Dadong-Xiaodaoliushui (大小倒流水) area outside the Great Wall, covering 200 hectares, and the area of the river gold area near Malanyu, covering 100 hectares, are the largest mining areas. These two mining fields, Dadong-Xiaodaoliushui, are licensed and mined by the Jibei Company, while the Malanyu river gold is mined by Zhang and Xing. Gold production has always been very high. In November last year, Japanese people, accompanied by traitors, went to survey the area. Less than a month later, dozens of workers were dispatched to work. The Jibei Company and the Malanyu Xing-Zhang mine owners fled to the interior during the war, so they did not know that they were being mined by the Japanese and puppet personnel. It was not until the end of last year that they learned the truth and the Jibei Company joined forces with other mining rights holders to submit a report to the Hebei Industry Department, requesting the Foreign Ministry to protest to the Japanese side. After one or two months, nothing happened. Recently, Xing and Zhang, the owners of the Malanyu mining field, came to the province to appeal to the Industry Department, saying that Japanese ronin have recently gathered hundreds of workers to squeeze into the Dadong-Xiaodaoliushui and Malanyu mining fields, expanding their work, and there is a plan to organize a gold mining stock company. The local county magistrate, under the protection of the Japanese army, does not dare to express opposition, so he lets the Japanese and traitors carry out the mining. After receiving the two mine owners' appeals, the Industry Department immediately submitted them to the provincial government, which in turn consulted with the Foreign Ministry to handle the matter of the occupation of the Dadong-Xiaodaoliushui mining field by the Jibei Company. Xing and Zhang have not yet left Tianjin while waiting for the results. According to the two, there are dozens of serpentine mines, pyrite mines, fossil mines, and granite mines along the Great Wall. Previously, people had obtained mining rights with licenses, but now, due to the Japanese army stationed in our territory, all the mines have stopped working. The Japanese, guided by traitors, have come to various mines to investigate, with ambitious intentions. If the negotiations over the Dadong-Xiaodaoliushui and Malanyu mines are fruitless, then other mines will also be successively occupied by the Japanese for large-scale investment. According to reports, after the puppet emperor's proclamation of usurpation, he is scheduled to visit Malanyu on April 5 to perform ancestral rites and sweep the tombs. Minister Shen Ruilin of his puppet Palace Affairs Department will be dispatched to Malanyu in advance to arrange everything. The traitors believe this to be an unparalleled opportunity, and as a result, they have been actively active recently. The county magistrate and local officials are all under the instruction of the Japanese army to prepare for the welcome. (17th)

Songjiang 97

Robbery case at Zhangze has leads on the bandits. The county water patrol team previously dispatched patrol boats No. 3 and 4 to the Hougang area, where they apprehended bandits Cai Busheng and suspect Wu Sanlao. They were taken back to the team headquarters, where Team Leader Shen held a preliminary hearing. According to Cai Busheng, he is 35 years old, from Caijiadai, Tu 22, Jinshan. He used to trade pigs and rice. He knew Song Gengsheng and Zhang Ziming, who were previously captured. On the eighth day of the twelfth month of last year, he robbed a family of unknown surname in the north of Tinglin, pried open the back door, entered the house, and tied up the victim. However, the binding was too loose, and the victim escaped, sounding the alarm outside. They only stole 16 yuan and three bags of clothes, which were distributed at Wu Ayou's house. He recalled that at the end of November, ten people robbed two families north of Zhangze, carrying two sharp knives and an axe. They entered through the back door, burned the victim's beard with candles, and stole five bags of clothes and more than 400 yuan, which are still being distributed at Wu Ayou's house. In the twelfth month of last year, a family surnamed Zhang in Zhangze was also robbed. He did not know about other cases. Suspect Wu Sanlao confessed that he is 52 years old, living in Jiangbeidai, Tu 22, Jin County, and makes a living by farming. Alai and his adopted son do not engage in proper work. He knows Wu Ayou's mother intimately. One night at the end of November, he went to Ayou's house and saw many people outside, all of whom were robbers. He was not involved in any of it.

Suzhou 98

Truth of the Hengjing Murder Case Comes to Light

Zhang Heshang, a villager from Mujicun, Hengjing, died suddenly after being beaten by his neighbor Xu Shuiquan. After Wu Xu, the deceased's sister, and others reported the case to the police, accusing Zhang's death of being caused by Xu Shuiquan's crushing of his testicles, Xu was arrested and sent to the District Prosecutor's Office for interrogation and detention. Yesterday morning (19th) at 8:00 AM, Prosecutor Shen Bingrong, accompanied by clerk Zhu and coroner Mao, took a steamboat to the village for an examination. It was determined that the deceased's scrotum was ruptured, leading to his death. Many injuries were also found on his head and other parts of his body. It was also found that the deceased's residence and Xu Shuiquan's house were connected. The two houses were only separated by a layer of reed mats, with no walls. There was also a small door next to the reed mats, allowing the perpetrator to freely enter the room to commit the crime. After the examination, they returned to the city at 5:00 PM.

Zhong Guochang from Guangdong, 34 years old, came to Suzhou on the 17th, using the alias Zhang Ziqing. He stayed in room 26 of the hotel in the city. Haimen 100

Shen Huaiqing's Home Robbed

Shen Huaiqing, from Xiaoyin Township, District 10, is from a relatively well-off family. He was robbed once before, but because the loss was not significant, he did not report the case. Unexpectedly, at the third watch the night before, more than a dozen bandits came again, speaking in local dialects, holding shotguns and wooden sticks, etc., swarming in. They pointed the guns at Shen's chest, frightening him into silence, while overturning boxes and cabinets, searching at will. They were soon heard by the neighbors, who rang the alarm. The bandits then fired shots to demonstrate, fleeing to the northeast. After taking stock, the loss was about 300 yuan in silver, jewelry, cloth, etc.

Shen Chujiang's Beloved Son Kidnapped 101

Shen Chujiang, the head of Liuzhou Township, District 6, is in his fifties, thrifty and frugal, and has saved a little. He has only one son, named Fubao, who is 11 years old. Chujiang and his wife love him like a precious pearl. Unexpectedly, at about 10 PM the day before, seven or eight bandits suddenly came, speaking in mixed dialects, holding box guns, breaking down the door and entering. They twisted Chujiang and his wife, beat them severely, and demanded silver. Failing to obtain it, they kidnapped Fubao and left. Afterwards, Chujiang, out of deep love for his son, feared that it would lead to an accident, and has not yet reported the case for investigation.

Seventy-Year-Old Woman Buried in Fire Pit 102

Song Fuqi's house in Xiaoyin Township, District 10, caught fire the day before, because the embers in the stove were not extinguished, causing the fire to spread. At that time, the east wind was very strong, making rescue difficult. Three tiled houses and two thatched houses were completely reduced to ashes. Song's mother, Chen, who was already 70 years old, was trapped by the smoke and fire and could not escape. She was buried in the fire pit, her limbs falling off, charred black like charcoal, a tragic sight.

Mr. Hunt Discusses American Silver Policy 119

Increasing Difficulties for China

The "Great American Evening Post" reports that Mr. Hunt, who served as the Chief Clerk of the U.S. House of Representatives from 1918 to 1932, is currently traveling around the world. He recently visited Shanghai and spoke with leaders of the Chinese business and financial community about American silver legislation. He stated that proponents of this legislation believe that its result will greatly increase China's purchasing power. This is a big mistake. In fact, this move will not only fail to benefit the Chinese people, but will increase their difficulties. Therefore, the Chinese government should urgently find ways to suppress silver prices in the Chinese market. China's foreign trade has always been in a deficit position, with last year's deficit reaching more than 700 million. Therefore, China must suppress silver prices in order to become a country with a trade surplus, or at least ensure that exports are balanced with the annually increasing imports. If Washington does pass the silver legislation, then the Chinese government should immediately work to maintain its financial structure. There are three ways to do this: prohibiting silver exports, imposing heavy silver export taxes, or implementing the gold standard. He believes that President Roosevelt, after studying the international silver situation, will be able to reject the Congress's recommendation, and that after further consideration, Congress will not pass this bill.

The Xing Shi Steamer of the Sanbei Shipping Company Catches Fire in Hankou 120

The Rear Cargo Hold Burns for Two and a Half Hours

More Than 500 Pieces of Cotton Yarn Destroyed

The Sanbei Shipping Company in Shanghai received a telegram yesterday from its Hankou branch, stating that the Xing Shi steamer caught fire in the rear cargo hold at 12:30 AM, and was extinguished after three hours. A second telegram stated that after 12:30 AM, a fire was discovered in the rear cabin, and was extinguished after two hours. The cargo in the rear cabin, including cotton yarn, glass, and steel, was damaged, but the ship's hull was unharmed. After these two telegrams arrived in Shanghai, a third telegram was received, reporting that among the burned cargo in the rear cabin, there were 500 pieces of cotton yarn, half of which were burned, and the unburned ones were mostly waterlogged. The glass and hardware were also damaged, resulting in a huge loss. The details are explored and recorded below:

Not Yet Unloaded Upon Arrival in Hankou 121

The Xing Shi steamer departed from Shanghai on the 14th of this month, loaded with a large batch of goods bound for Hankou. It stopped at Wuhu, Anqing, Jiujiang, and other places along the way, where some goods were unloaded. When the ship arrived in Hankou on the 18th, it docked at the company's wharf. According to the usual practice, the hatches should have been opened for unloading that day, but because it was Sunday, the Jianghan Customs was closed, so unloading was postponed to yesterday, Monday. The steamer was scheduled to set sail from Hankou this morning to return to Shanghai.

Fire Breaks Out in the Cabin at Midnight 122

The dockworkers left because the ship was rescheduled to open the hatches on the 19th. Unexpectedly, at midnight that night, at 12:50 AM on the 19th, smoke suddenly billowed from the rear cabin of the ship. Most of the crew members were already asleep. When the watchman on the ship discovered the fire and urgently reported it to the captain, the flames had already emerged from the cabin. Upon receiving the news, the captain immediately gathered all the ship's workers, and first used the ship's firefighting equipment to fight the fire. Fortunately, the ship was docked at the wharf and there were many people available to help fight the fire.

Many Passengers and Goods Burned 123

The Xing Shi steamer this time loaded Shanghai goods, mostly cotton yarn, piece goods, hardware, cigarettes, and glass. The rear cabin contained steel at the bottom, glass in the middle, and cotton yarn piece goods on top. Once the fire broke out, it immediately spread to the yarn cloth. Although the steel and glass were not burned, they were damaged significantly. Fortunately, each cabin had iron bulkheads, preventing the fire from spreading to the middle cabin. It was not until two hours later that the flames were extinguished. After flooding the cabin with water, the fire was completely extinguished. The Shanghai office has telegraphed the ship's captain to investigate the matter thoroughly.

Li Liejun Admitted to Hospital 124

Blood Pressure Worsens Again

The Xin Xin News Agency reports that Li Liejun, a member of the Central Committee who has been living in Shanghai in retirement, originally planned to go to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee after the Fujian Incident was settled, but was unable to do so due to suffering from high blood pressure. Shanghai Telephone Company Gradually Laying Off Employees 125

More Than 40 People Laid Off in February

Workers Feel the Pain of Unemployment

The Shen Shi News Agency reports that the Shanghai Telephone Company, after purchasing all the assets of the China and Foreign Telephone Company on August 5, 1930, and converting to automatic telephones, has completed the conversion in less than 20 months. At that time, due to the high demand for employees, it temporarily recruited hundreds of people from various sources to speed up the process. Now that the conversion is complete, there is very little need for these employees. Since the end of January this year, it has gradually laid off employees, with more than 40 people being laid off in February alone. These employees, who have received specialized training, feel the pain of unemployment once they are laid off.

The Shen Shi News Agency reporter specifically visited Mr. Perry, the British Director of the Business Department of the company, to inquire about the details. According to him, the employees being laid off were those who were temporarily recruited during the conversion to automatic telephones. Now that the company's need for labor has decreased, it has no choice but to gradually lay them off in order to reduce expenses. However, the laid-off employees are still given lifetime pensions or additional preferential wages for several months to show compassion. Mr. Perry also stated that the Shanghai Telephone Company belongs to the International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation, which has more than 90 companies around the world specializing in electrical communications, and has an international character. The Shanghai Telephone Company is now one part of it. When the company implemented the great project of converting to automatic telephone exchanges, it recruited specialized personnel and other employees from all over the world, in large numbers. Now that the project has been completed, most of them have been sent back to various parts of the world, not just a portion of local employees being laid off.

The Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Society Undertakes to Repair the Two Gates of the Guangcheng Dike 130

Personnel Have Already Departed

The Guangcheng Dike in Huaining, Anhui Province, has been silted up for many years and has repeatedly suffered from floods. The people are poor and resources are exhausted, with more than ten thousand people facing starvation and unable to survive. The Chinese and Western directors of the Congren Bureau in Anqing and the members of the Dike Works Committee have repeatedly appealed to the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Society on Renji Road in Shanghai, and have sent representatives to explain the situation in person. Now that the water has receded, urgent repairs are needed, otherwise there will be no relief, and the more than ten thousand survivors, the young and strong will become bandits, and the old and weak will fill the ditches. Their words were very urgent. However, the entire project requires a huge amount of money. The society, facing limited donations and financial difficulties, had to find a way to help in the most impossible of situations. They勉爲擔任undertook a portion of the dike, repairing the north and south gates. The project will be overseen by Bishop Han of the Wuhu branch, and the supervision of all matters will be undertaken by Mr. Zheng Shouchang, a special commissioner dispatched by the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Society. He departed last night with the representatives of the province, Chuan Shunsheng, Wu Qingcen, and Yang Jianquan.

The Mechanical Industries Association Requests Mediation on the Sichuan Guild's Opposition to Price Increases in Shanghai-Chongqing Shipping 132

Caring Only for Personal Gain

Blocking the Transportation of Domestic Goods to Sichuan

The Shanghai Mechanical Domestic Goods Factory Federation, according to a letter from the Preparatory Office of the Chongqing Su Goods Guild in Shanghai, states that "Our guild has always been responsible for purchasing Chinese and foreign miscellaneous goods in Shanghai and transporting them to Sichuan for sale. In recent years, we have resisted foreign goods and promoted domestic goods. Our guild's patriotism has always been second to none. We have completely switched from selling foreign goods to selling domestic goods. Each year we purchase more than ten million yuan worth of foreign and Chinese miscellaneous goods in Shanghai, selling no less than seven or eight million yuan of sugar porcelain, cotton textiles, silk textiles, wool textiles, rubber products, cosmetics, thermos bottles, umbrellas, toothbrushes, glassware, steel products, bakelite products, toys, lamps, etc., from your members' factories. We have always used the Jiang Tai Gu shipping companies for transportation, and the freight rates have been reasonable, so transportation has been smooth. Unexpectedly, in mid-February this year, the Minsheng, Jardine Matheson, Taikoo, Jiang Tai, Sanbei, and Guangyao companies, without knowing who initiated it, suddenly signed an agreement to form a cooperative alliance similar to a trust, increasing freight rates by 80 to 200-300% compared to last winter. Some rates have even increased six or seven times compared to the old regulations for Chongqing shipping. The extraordinary increase in freight rates is unheard of in Chinese ports and unique in the world. Relying only on the limited vision of one or two ignorant individuals, they arbitrarily divide domestic goods with low costs into grades, stipulate measuring scales, and collect freight rates ranging from 2.5 to 1.25 yuan per cubic foot. The freight rates exceed the cost of the goods or account for 70-80% of the purchase price. Countless goods are transported to Sichuan, where they must be subject to customs duties and local taxes of 20%, exchange rates of 15-16%, and miscellaneous taxes of 2%. Any goods priced at one yuan in Shanghai must be sold for more than two yuan in Sichuan just to break even. At present, the people are impoverished, warlords are rampant, and the communists are causing disturbances. How can the people of Sichuan afford to buy goods at increased prices? If we insist on transporting all the goods with the newly increased freight rates, no one will avoid suffering great losses. Therefore, our members have decided that there is no way to transport domestic goods from your members' factories except to stop transportation. However, manufacturers in various countries hope that we can quickly transport their goods to Sichuan for promotion, so that the economy can be active, and they are also deeply enthusiastic. However, the shipping companies only care about personal profit, ignoring whether or not the promotion of domestic goods is hindered, and stubbornly raise freight rates. This is tantamount to blocking the main sales channels for domestic goods to Sichuan. The annual sales of several million yuan from your members' factories will be cut off, which is no small matter for the future of promoting domestic goods. In addition to attaching a comparative table of the current freight rates increased by various shipping companies, we are writing to you to verify the matter and allow us to transfer it to the Social Affairs Bureau to convene mediation and re-establish appropriate freight rates to facilitate the transportation and promotion of domestic goods. This is truly in the public interest." It is heard that the association, because the matter concerns monopolizing freight rates and hindering domestic goods, has forwarded it to the Social Affairs Bureau to convene mediation.
