The Shanghai Telephone Bureau Takes Over the Minhang District's Commercial Telephone Service 133

Pan Zhongjia, the Shanghai County Magistrate and concurrently the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Fifth District, considering that the county government has relocated and various undertakings are developing rapidly, and that the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway is open to traffic, making Minhang District a transportation hub between east and west, while the original commercially operated (Shanghai-Minhang Long-Distance Bus Company concurrently operated) telephone service has simple equipment and the cable lines are insufficient for the entire county's application, Pan personally came to Shanghai and negotiated with Xu Xueyu, the Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, to transfer the county's telephone service to government operation. Pan also obtained the consent of the Long-Distance Bus Company.

Total Funds: The procedures for transferring the commercial telephone rights to government operation have been decided by both parties in the previous days. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau estimates that the total cost of reconstructing the county's telephone system is approximately 8,000 to 9,000 yuan. Whether the Shanghai Telephone Bureau will fully bear this cost in the future, or whether the county government and local gentry and merchants will raise funds to subsidize half of the cost, is still under negotiation.

Survey Project: The project of reconstructing the telephone pole line between Shanghai and Minhang is being planned by the Engineering Department. It is planned to first install two pairs of total return lines during the initial stage. The telephone pole line will start from the Shanghai Telephone Bureau headquarters at Dananmen, and run straight along Xietu Road through Zhuanqiao to Minhang, and a branch bureau will be established in Minhang. In order to determine the electricity fee project and the total amount of funds, the bureau will send engineers and surveyors to conduct a survey within days. Once the fundraising procedures for both parties are resolved, construction will begin.

The Barbers' Association Petitions the Municipal Party Department 134

Barbershop Employees Should Join the Trade Association

Wei Guoyi, the standing member of the Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Barbers' Trade Association, submitted a document to the Municipal Party Department, stating that "We are submitting this document to present that barbershop employees should join the trade association and report on the situation of Zhang Dafu preventing the meeting from being held, hoping that you will understand our difficulties and approve the establishment on a designated date. In the industry, the distribution of profits between the boss and the employees is mostly based on a four-six split, with daily settlements, and there are no disagreements. This has been a long-standing practice. Moreover, most of the barbershop owners work hard from morning to night, and never express themselves as bosses. And 30-40% of the barbershop employees are shareholders, but they also work the same way and operate together. Since there is no class distinction between the boss and the employees, how can we distinguish between labor and capital? Even if someone is a boss in the morning and an employee in the evening, the situation is special and changes rapidly. It is clear that this cannot be compared with ordinary companies and firms. It is also clear that the boss and the employees cannot take different paths when organizing groups. If the barbershop owners organize a trade association and the barbershop employees organize a labor union, where would those who are both bosses and employees go? If both parties join, it is inevitable that they will both suffer. This may also conflict with the provisions of the Industrial and Commercial Law. For example, in teahouses and bathhouses, there are barbershop chair positions, and there are also bag carriers and porters, etc. In name, they can all be called bosses and employees, but how should they be treated? It is easy to make them hesitate. We ask for separate instructions. In the past, there were groups organized by barbershop owners alone. In 1928, it was called the Business People's Association, and in 1931, it was called the Trade Association. Because the barbershop employees could not participate, it caused great disputes. As a result, both sides were hurt, and it was too late to regret. They were either dissolved informally or ordered to be revoked. In May of last year, the Gao Yatou Tragedy Association was completely cooperated by the boss and the employees, so they were able to achieve the final victory. Therefore, whether the barbershop employees should join the trade association or not, we can learn from the past and present. The advantages and disadvantages are clear, and there is no need to repeat them. Therefore, in the membership list submitted by our association, the term "Director" (i.e., barbershop owner) and "Employee" are clearly indicated as boss and employee cooperation. Now, the barbershop owners and employees in the city urgently need the establishment of a trade association, and they long for it like a drought longs for rain. We are submitting this document to express our sincerity, hoping that you will understand our difficulties and approve the establishment on a designated date. It would be a great kindness. We respectfully submit this to the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special City Party Department."

Jiahe Crew Members Discuss Along-the-Way Sightings 135

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiahe steamer arrived in Shanghai yesterday. A reporter met with the crew members, who told of assisting the rescue of the Hai Shun and discovering a large ship in distress off the Taizhou Islands. A summary of the situation is recorded below:

Assisting in the Rescue of the Hai Shun 136

The British steamer Hai Shun and the Jiahe steamer both departed from Fuzhou. The Hai Shun left four hours earlier. When the Jiahe sailed to the waters off the White Dog Island, the Hai Shun had already run aground on the reef. Because of the fog in the Fujian waters, the Hai Shun sailed outside the Seven Sisters Islands off the White Dog Island to avoid danger. Unexpectedly, the ship was forced by the wind and waves to run aground on the White Dog Island. The passengers were rescued by a small vessel from the Minhai Customs. When the Jiahe arrived, it anchored there to prevent theft. When the Taikoo Ninghai steamer arrived, the Jiahe sailed to Shanghai. The Hai Shun's hull was completely broken and the ship could not be salvaged.

Discovery of a Ship in Distress 137

On the 18th, the Jiahe steamer was passing through the waters off the Taizhou Islands. It caught a glimpse of a large ship aground in the bay of Haitan, a place called Dacheng Mountain. Because there are so many reefs in this area, this ship was grounded, perhaps due to fog and misnavigation, or accidentally entered this bay. The ship was very large, with a yellow smokestack. Because the Jiahe was far away, it could not see the ship's name. According to the crew members, it seemed to be flying an American flag. The Jiahe sent a telegram to inquire but received no reply. Later, it saw a Japanese ship anchored outside the ship, providing assistance, so the Jiahe sailed to Shanghai. It is said that this ship is a Japanese ship, but it cannot be proven. It is still aground among the reefs.

Transporting Soldiers and Civilians 138

This time, the Jiahe steamer carried 328 foreign refugees sent from Xiamen Public Security Bureau to Shanghai, and 177 scattered soldiers, who were transported to Shanghai for dispersal. The Min authorities, with the approval of the China Merchants Bureau, had the Jiahe steamer transport them to Shanghai. Yesterday, when the ship arrived in Shanghai, the bureau had already notified the Public Security Bureau to send police to take care of them.

The Two Courts Stipulate Security Measures and Rules for Observers 142

Jiangsu Higher Court Second Branch, Shanghai First Special District Local Court, Proclamation No. 3004: It is noted that litigation in both courts is extremely frequent, and the court premises are relatively narrow, resulting in a large number of people entering and exiting, inevitably causing crowding and disorder, which not only affects appearances but also easily causes accidents. We have increased the number of security guards to direct and maintain order. The following simple rules for security guards to maintain order and simple rules for issuing observer tickets are hereby formulated for compliance, and will be implemented on the 21st of this month. In addition to ordering police officers to comply, this announcement is hereby issued for general knowledge. The simple rules for security guards to maintain order are as follows: (1) The west gate of this court is not allowed to pass through except for cars leaving the court. Anyone entering the court from the east gate of this court, except for staff and police officers of the two courts and prisons, detectives, lawyers, those with badges and uniforms that can be identified, or those familiar to the security guards, must be questioned by the security guards on duty to ascertain their identity before being allowed to enter, and shall be handled in accordance with the following provisions: (a) If they are guests, they should be directed to the reception room to present their business cards; (b) If they are litigants or witnesses, they should be asked to present their summons or court rescheduling slips. If they are witnesses brought by the litigants or other people involved in the case who come to court voluntarily without a summons, they must be questioned in detail or asked to provide relevant proof and directed to the waiting room or which courtroom; (c) If they are observers, they should be instructed to go to the observer ticket issuing office to obtain a ticket; (d) If they are going to the prison to visit or deliver goods, or to the receiving and dispatching office, cashier's office, or inquiry office to submit documents, pay fees, or ask questions, they should be directed to a specific location; (e) If they are merchants who come to the court to deliver or order goods for transactions, they should be directed to the general affairs office of each department; (f) No one may stay in the court after their business is completed. (2) Except for litigants and observers entering the court of each criminal division, who are responsible for inspection by the judicial police on duty, and the civil division of the High Court and the Fourth Civil Division of the Local Court, which are temporarily inspected by the court clerk, the other civil divisions are responsible for inspection by the security guards. Anyone who is not a litigant in the relevant court or who does not have an observer ticket is not allowed to enter the court. "Simple rules for issuing observer tickets:" (1) Anyone who wishes to observe the court proceedings of the two courts, except for special observers and those who have long-term observer passes, must obtain a daily observer ticket. (2) An observer ticket issuing office is set up inside the east gate of this court. Each day, tickets are prepared and issued in accordance with the number of observer seats in each court without charge. Tickets will stop being issued once the number is full. (3) Those requesting an observer ticket should first state which court and case they wish to observe so that the court name can be filled in. (4) After obtaining a ticket, observers should immediately go to the courtroom indicated on the ticket and hand the ticket to the bailiff or court clerk for verification before entering the courtroom to observe. They should leave immediately after the hearing and hand the ticket back to the original verifying bailiff or court clerk. They must not stay in the court. If they wish to observe another hearing, they must follow the previous procedure and obtain another ticket. (5) Observers should abide by these simple rules and the rules for observers. March 17, Republic of China Year 23. Court President Shen Jiayi, Court President Guo Yunguan.

Twenty-Four Chinese Cigarette Factories Jointly Petition for the Amendment of the Tax System 146

The Number of Chinese Merchants Decreased From 160 to 40 or 50

Domestic Huanggang and Junzhou Tobacco Leaves are Completely Unsalable

The Chinese cigarette factories, including the Minzhong Cigarette Company, China Huaxing Cigarette Company, Youli Cigarette Factory, Asia Tobacco Company, Yonghe Tobacco Company, Yuxin Cigarette Factory, China Dada Cigarette Factory, Xinmin Cigarette Factory, Jiuyi Cigarette Company, Huamei Tobacco Co., Ltd., Jinshan Cigarette Factory, Huaqing Tobacco Company, Huafu Cigarette Factory, Jinshataiji Tobacco Company, Delong Cigarette Factory, Shanghai Cigarette Company, China Southeast Tobacco Company, Jiangzhe Cigarette Company, Zhongnan Cigarette Factory, Zhuxing Cigarette Factory, Kefu Cigarette Company, Zhonghe Cigarette Company, etc., totaling 24 companies, have jointly submitted a petition stating that the current cigarette tax rate treats Chinese and foreign merchants unfairly. They request a prompt amendment to provide relief. The petition was submitted to the Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry, and the Taxation Department. The petition reads: "Regarding the current cigarette tax rate, which treats Chinese and foreign merchants unfairly, we request a prompt amendment to provide relief. The cigarette unified tax is currently set as a two-tier tax by order of the Ministry of Finance. The first tier is for cigarettes with a selling price of over 300 yuan per case, with a tax of 160 yuan. The second tier is for cigarettes with a selling price of 300 yuan or less per case, with a tax of 80 yuan. The selling price in non-factory locations can be relaxed by 20 yuan, etc. During this period of national construction and bandit suppression, the government is raising funds to build the country, suppress bandits, and secure the people. We, under the leadership of the National Government, dare not refuse to increase the burden for the sake of loving the country and the party. However, the tax rate is inappropriately high or low. We believe that it is unacceptable. The level of taxation is closely related to the prosperity and decline of commerce. If the tax rate is good, the people will not feel the pain even if the tax is heavy. If the tax rate is bad, the people will not be able to make a living even if the tax is light. The distinction between good and bad lies in two points: 1. Whether the burden is equal; 2. Whether it can protect domestic commerce. However, the tax rate set by the Ministry of Finance this time is the opposite of these two principles. This must be reported to our people-loving government. The cigarette unified tax was established in 1929 and has been revised three times in November 1930, February 1931, and March 1932. From July 1929 to November 1930, it was the era of seven-tier tax. From November 1930 to February 1931, it was the era of the old three-tier tax. From February 1931 to March 1932, it was the era of the new three-tier tax. From March 1932 to the present, it has been the era of the two-tier tax. The tax rate has been increasing each time. Before 1912, there was only one British and American company in the cigarette industry. After 1912, Chinese merchants, calling for national goods, emerged one after another, and there is today. Generally, upper and middle-grade cigarettes are mostly made by British and American companies, while Chinese merchants mostly produce lower-grade cigarettes. Upper and middle-grade cigarettes mostly use American tobacco leaves, while lower-grade cigarettes mostly use domestic American tobacco leaves and native leaves. Because of the difference in tax rates and the difference in upper, middle, and lower-grade products, British and American companies and Chinese merchants often occupy opposing positions. If the tax rate is divided into many tiers, the burden on upper, middle, and lower-grade cigarettes will vary according to the quality of the cigarettes, so the burden on lower-grade cigarettes is lighter, and Chinese merchants are in a favorable position, and domestic tobacco leaves are also sold well. If the tax rate is divided into fewer tiers, the burden on upper, middle, and lower-grade cigarettes will not be very different, or even the burden on lower-grade cigarettes will exceed that of upper and middle-grade cigarettes by one or two times, so the burden on upper and middle-grade cigarettes is lighter, British and American companies are in a favorable position, and domestic tobacco leaves are also unsalable. According to past experience, the seven-tier tax is most beneficial to Chinese merchants, followed by the three-tier tax, and the two-tier tax clearly favors British and American companies, and Chinese merchants have no power to resist. Therefore, in the era of the seven-tier tax, there were a total of 150 or 160 Chinese merchants. With the implementation of the two-tier tax, they closed down one after another, and now there are only 40 or 50 left. In recent years, the number of sales has also decreased sharply, and many have suffered losses. At the beginning of the 1932 tax reform, there was opposition because they knew that the treatment was unfair and they were unable to resist. However, the Ministry of Finance insisted on a trial basis and did not approve the revision. After more than a year, the drawbacks have become more apparent. If we separately calculate the sales volume and tax payment of British and American companies and other cigarette companies over the years, it is truly shocking to see the depth of the harm to Chinese merchants and the weight of the preferential treatment to British and American companies. The unified cigarette tax stamps used by British and American companies and other cigarette companies, as well as the tax payments of each cigarette company, are recorded in detail in the Unified Tax Gazette and the Tax Gazette. Now, based on this information, we have separately prepared a comparative table of the unified cigarette tax stamps used by British and American cigarette companies and other cigarette companies in the era of the three-tier tax and the era of the two-tier tax, as well as a comparative table of tax payments. First, let's talk about the use of stamps. According to the unified tax regulations, every 50,000 cigarettes is considered a large case, and one stamp is affixed. Therefore, the number of stamps used is the number of cases of cigarettes sold. In the era of the three-tier tax, the average number for British and American companies was 30,472, and the average number for other companies was 68,422. The sales volume of British and American companies was only 40% of that of other companies, less than 50%. In the era of the two-tier tax, the average number for British and American companies was 48,808, and the average number for other companies was 44,323. The sales volume of British and American companies has exceeded that of other companies by 4,485. Alas, in one year, British and American companies have made such rapid progress, and Chinese merchants have declined so much. People with conscience will be shocked and lose their courage. Next, let's talk about the tax payments. In the era of the three-tier tax, the average amount for British and American cigarette companies was 2,417,403.822 yuan, and the average amount for other cigarette companies was 2,006,252.647 yuan. The burden on British and American companies was 410,000 yuan more than that of Chinese merchants. In the era of the two-tier tax, the average amount for British and American cigarette companies was 2,726,392.522 yuan, and the amount for other cigarette companies was 2,554,466.996 yuan. The burden on British and American companies was only 170,000 yuan more than that of Chinese merchants. Comparing these two tables, in the era of the three-tier tax, although the sales volume of British and American companies was less than 50% of that of Chinese merchants, the monthly tax payment was 410,000 yuan more than that of Chinese merchants, because the quality of the cigarettes was good and the selling price was high, so the tax was also heavy. Now, with the change to the two-tier tax, the sales volume of British and American companies, which was less than 50% of that of Chinese merchants, has increased to more than 100%, and the tax payment has decreased to only 170,000 yuan per month. This is the result of the tax reduction on upper-grade cigarettes and the tax increase on lower-grade cigarettes. Therefore, the burden on British and American companies has been sharply reduced, while the burden on Chinese merchants has doubled. No wonder that in one year, British and American companies have made rapid progress, while the closure of Chinese merchants has accounted for almost two-thirds of the total. The government loves and protects domestic businesses, how can it make such a bad plan? The government may not be clear about the interests. Also, the fifth meeting minutes of the Tax Design Committee, which was recorded in the sixth issue of the first volume of the Tax Gazette in December 1932, stated "This year's tax increase is only 27 percent more than last year's average tax rate, and the sales volume has decreased by more than 20 percent." This shows that the people's burden has increased as a result of the tax increase, and the government has not received corresponding benefits. Because lower-grade cigarettes are heavily taxed, poor people buy and smoke illicit cigarettes. The Tax Design Committee has obtained the answer in the statistics, and it has been published in the meeting minutes and in the gazette. This autumn, Director Xie, representing Minister Song, invited Chinese and foreign cigarette merchants to a meeting and declared that there would be no tax increase within a year. This has been widely heard. The Tax Design Committee is the only agency that designs taxes for the government. The Minister of Finance and the Director of the Taxation Department are the chief officers in charge of the cigarette tax. The ink is still wet, and the words are still echoing, but suddenly there is talk of a tax increase. It is inevitable to contradict themselves and repeat the mistakes of the two-tier tax in 1932. This is even worse, with more tax reduction for upper-grade cigarettes and more tax increase for lower-grade cigarettes. This is more evil than the old two-tier tax and cannot be abolished immediately. Why do we say this? The determination of the tax rate, in ancient and modern times, at home and abroad, is always calculated based on the value of hundreds of items. For example, the current tax on alcohol and tobacco is set at 20% of the value. When the cigarette tax was in the seven-tier system, it was approximately 32.5% of the value. The tax rate currently set by the Ministry of Finance, is it close to % of the value? Lower-grade cigarettes, with a selling price of 120 yuan per case, used to have a tax of more than 55 yuan, and the cost was 65 yuan. If the value is 65 yuan, the tax is 55 yuan, which is more than 90% of the value. Now it is changed to 80 yuan, that is, if the value is 65 yuan, the tax is 80 yuan, which is more than 120% of the value. Upper-grade cigarettes above 300 yuan are now also taxed at the second level. Taking the selling price of 300 yuan as an example, after deducting the tax of 80 yuan, the cost is 220 yuan. If the value is 220 yuan, the tax is 80 yuan, which is 36% of the value. For these upper-grade cigarettes with a selling price of 300 yuan, the second-level tax last year was still 95 yuan, that is, if the value is 205 yuan, the tax is 95 yuan, which is still 47% of the value. From this point of view, the result of this year's tax reform is that the lower-grade cigarettes have increased from 90% of the value to more than 120% of the value, and the upper-grade cigarettes have decreased from 47% of the value to 36% of the value. All those who can afford to smoke cigarettes with a selling price of 300 yuan per case are wealthy merchants and have the ability to pay taxes, and the burden should be heavy. Those who smoke cigarettes with a selling price of 120 yuan per case are poor people and lack the ability to pay taxes, and the burden should be light. If the government wants to raise funds, it should choose those who have the ability to pay taxes and impose heavy taxes to increase national income. Now, instead of doing this, it imposes a heavy tax of more than 120% of the value on those who have no ability to pay taxes, and imposes a light tax of only 36% of the value on those who have the ability to pay taxes. The difference in the burden is so great. Why does the government love wealthy merchants and give them a tax reduction when raising funds? Why does it hate poor people and impose heavy taxes on them? If we talk about the Chinese and foreign merchants in the cigarette industry, most of those who make upper-grade cigarettes are British and American companies, and all those who make lower-grade cigarettes are Chinese merchants, as we have said in detail before. If the tax on upper-grade cigarettes is reduced and the tax on lower-grade cigarettes is increased, it is equivalent to reducing the tax on foreign merchants and increasing the tax on Chinese merchants. Chinese merchants' capital and talents are not as good as foreign merchants, and they often fail in business wars. Unfortunately, the tax rate set this time is that the burden on foreign merchants is only 36% of the value, while the burden on Chinese merchants is more than 120% of the value, which is more than three times. This is tantamount to tying the hands and feet of Chinese merchants and waiting for foreign merchants to attack with planes and cannons. How can Chinese merchants not close down one after another in this kind of business war? Political organizations must also love their own people. However, the tax rate is so upside down. The merchants think about this day and night. I don't know why the government loves foreign merchants and gives them the benefit of tax reduction, and hates Chinese merchants and imposes heavy taxes on them. Now, let's discuss this fairly. Does the government want to value the cigarette at %. The current value is 120%, which puts the cigarette industry to death and is unacceptable. But if the government insists on implementing this tax system, the upper and middle-grade cigarettes should have an equal increase to show fairness. For the convenience of calculation, we also use a selling price of 120 yuan for lower-grade cigarettes, divided into three grades: For a selling price of 120 yuan, the tax used to be 55 yuan, and the cost was 65 yuan. Now it is changed to 120 yuan of the value, then the cost is 65 yuan, the tax is 80 yuan, and the selling price should be 145 yuan, which is the third grade. The middle-grade cigarette, calculated as the lower-grade cigarette plus half of the cost, then a selling price of 217 yuan and 50 cents should be set to a tax of 129 yuan, which is a cost of 97 yuan and 50 cents, and a tax of 120 yuan, which is the second grade. The upper-grade cigarette, calculated as the lower-grade cigarette plus the cost, then a selling price of 290 yuan should be set to a tax of 160 yuan, which is a cost of 130 yuan, and a tax of 160 yuan, which is the first grade. (Table omitted) If we follow the above table, the tax rate will be the same for upper, middle, and lower-grade cigarettes, which is more fair. According to the figures, the government's tax revenue can also increase by tens of millions of yuan per year. However, the government is not willing to adopt this because it is concerned that the upper and middle-grade cigarettes do not have the ability to bear the value of 120%, and if it is implemented, all cigarette factories in the country will close down. If the upper and middle-grade cigarettes cannot bear the value of 120%, can the lower-grade cigarettes bear it? The government knows how to protect the upper and middle-grade cigarettes of foreign merchants, but the government does not even think about protecting the lower-grade cigarettes of Chinese merchants and intends to put them to death. Or some may say that the cigarettes above 300 yuan are now taxed at the first level and are taxed at 160 yuan, which is not heavy. But the sales of cigarettes above 300 yuan are extremely rare, and they are allowed to be relaxed by 20 yuan in non-factory locations. In essence, the first-level tax is just a decoration of the tax system, and in fact, only one-level tax is implemented. Cigarettes around 300 yuan are only taxed at 36% of the value. The fortunate foreign merchants have obtained this low tax of 36% of the value, and the sales will inevitably increase, and a lot of money will be bundled and taken away. The unfortunate Chinese merchants bear a heavy tax of 120% of the value, which is more than three times the amount of foreign merchants. How can they compete in the market? The only way is to be defeated one by one and call out under the iron hooves of foreign merchants, and all will perish. Not only that, but the Chinese merchant-produced mid- and low-grade cigarettes, the tobacco leaves used, are either American tobacco leaves produced in Henan, Shandong, and Anhui, or domestic tobacco leaves such as Huanggang, Junzhou, Dengsu, Song, and Xinchang. The annual output of American and local leaves is approximately 150 million pounds, and the average selling price is 20 cents per pound. Farmers' annual income is approximately 30 million yuan. The government's smoked tobacco tax is 4 yuan and 15 cents per 100 catties, and the tax revenue is approximately 4.5 million to 5 million yuan. The remaining domestic tobacco leaves, such as Huanggang and Junzhou, are produced annually at approximately 100 million pounds. The income of the government and farmers is also worth one-third of the American and local leaves. In the era of the seven-tier tax, the tax rate and the value of the cigarettes were the standards for each other, so domestic tobacco leaves were most sold well. When the three-tier tax system was changed, the tax on upper-grade cigarettes was cheap, and the tax on lower-grade cigarettes was expensive. Therefore, the sales of American leaves took away half of the domestic tobacco leaves. Last year, the unified tax was changed to two levels, and lower-grade cigarettes became more difficult to survive. Therefore, domestic tobacco leaves such as Huanggang and Junzhou were completely unsalable. This year, compared with last year, the prices of tobacco leaves such as Xuzhou, Weixian, and Fengyang were high and the prices were low, but there were fewer buyers. This was also affected by the heavy tax on lower-grade cigarettes. The prosperity and decline of lower-grade cigarettes are closely related to the sales of domestic tobacco leaves. If lower-grade cigarettes disappear from the market due to heavy taxes, the sales of domestic tobacco leaves will be cut off. Not only will the government's tobacco tax suffer a great loss, but the rural areas will also go bankrupt. Therefore, heavy taxes on lower-grade cigarettes are tantamount to choking the tax source and directly harming Chinese merchants and indirectly harming tobacco farmers. During this period of rural bankruptcy and rampant red bandits, can the government not consider the millions of tobacco farmers and put them to death for the sake of the fish? All of the above statements are clearly seen and understood by children. We merchants would never have expected such a tax rate to come from our people-loving government. We still request that you change to the seven-tier tax based on the principle of equal burden and protection of Chinese merchants, so that the tax rate is determined by the height of the selling price of upper, middle, and lower-grade cigarettes. At a minimum, you must ensure that the burden is equal, so that Chinese merchants have an equal opportunity to develop their business and are not oppressed by foreign merchants, so that there is a glimmer of hope. At this time of difficult situation, the government needs money everywhere, and the people should increase their burden. What we don't want to see is that the tax on upper-grade cigarettes is reduced, the tax on lower-grade cigarettes is increased, foreign merchants get light taxes, Chinese merchants bear heavy taxes, foreigners laugh and Chinese merchants cry. Minister Kong used to be the Minister of Industry and took care of Chinese merchants in every possible way. This time, he took office as the Minister of Finance. Due to the shortage of military and political expenses, he hurriedly discussed the tax increase, or he did not make a deep consideration, and the original plan stated that it was a trial run, which is enough to see that there are still doubts about this tax rate. We merchants live and eat here and know it deeply. We have true knowledge and insights about the bad tax rate and have statistical figures to rely on. We dare not sit idly by and watch the social economy and our own business perish. Therefore, we dare to state in detail that the Executive Yuan is responsible for leading the administration, the Ministry of Finance and the Taxation Department are the competent authorities, and the Ministry of Industry has the obligation to protect Chinese merchants. They must not sit idly by. I think they will be able to determine the average tax rate based on the heart of justice, so that Chinese merchants are not restrained, and the entire social economy is affected by it. The Legislative Yuan has the power to discuss and decide on the tax rate, and should have a fair proposition. I can't bear to abandon my duties and let the merchants be in distress and without hope. Urgent words, I hope to be adopted. In addition to submitting separately, I hereby submit to the Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry, and the Taxation Department.

Appalling Import of Japanese Agar-Agar 147

Recently, 500 Crates Arrived in Shanghai

Agar-agar, also known as "liangcai" or "dongfen," which we use daily in vegetarian dishes, has various other applications besides being a vegetable. In the summer, it's used to make jelly; Western restaurants use it for jellies like banana jelly and rose jelly. Agar-agar is the main ingredient, widely used and sold in huge quantities. Although the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong in our country produce it, the products are poor, and the color is not white, far inferior to Japanese products. Therefore, for decades, the agar-agar we used all came from Japan, one of the Japanese people's specialty products. Since the May Fourth Movement, the boycott of Japanese goods has been enthusiastic, and the import of Japanese agar-agar began to decline slightly. Subsequently, due to the September 18th and January 28th incidents, the import of agar-agar to China declined even further. Japanese agar-agar manufacturers suffered significant losses. Unexpectedly, the patriotic spirit of the Chinese people has weakened, and recently, the boycott movement has gradually been forgotten. Japanese people are taking advantage of the opportunity, and Japanese goods are being imported again in a steady stream. Taking agar-agar as an example, recently, another 500 crates have been transported to China, divided into three batches and transported to Shanghai. Besides the first batch already sold in this city, the remaining two or three batches have also been successively transported to various countries for sale. Although patriotic youths in this city are paying close attention to this matter, unscrupulous merchants are blinded by profit and spare no effort to promote the sale of enemy goods by all means.

Highest Reached 81 Degrees

Since the beginning of spring in this city, the weather has been cold and warm alternately, resulting in influenza and childhood smallpox almost everywhere. On the 17th, it gradually turned mild. The day before yesterday, the sky was clear, and the gentle breeze was pleasant, with a hint of mid-spring weather. Yesterday was even warmer, and the Fahrenheit thermometer rose to 81 degrees, resembling early summer weather. Most of the citizens have changed into cotton-lined clothing, which seems to be very beneficial to the ripening of spring crops in the fields.

The First District Party Department of the Shanghai Special Municipality, because the Shanghai Municipal Public Shanghai Hospital has mishandled the management of patients and disregarded human life, has submitted a request to the Municipal Party Department to forward to the Municipal Government for the removal of the hospital director, Zhou Chuliang. The text of the submission is transcribed as follows: "Submission for forwarding. According to the report from the 37th sub-district, according to the report from citizen Ren Xincai, requesting a thorough investigation of the Nanshi Public Shanghai Hospital for disregarding human life, and forwarding to the superior Party Department for prompt investigation to uphold humanity and quell public outrage. The Nanshi Shanghai Hospital is the only public hospital in this city, with a long history and trusted by the citizens. However, since Zhou Chuliang became the acting director, the management has been poor, the hospital affairs have been neglected, and public opinion is buzzing, which is a hidden worry for the future of the hospital. However, rumors outside say that the death of the bitter child Yu A'san was not due to incurable illness, but because he was

the weakness of the hospital's poor management and neglect of human life. Under the bright sky and white sun, in a dignified public hospital, such illegal incidents occurred, and there is such a director who manages poorly and disregards human life. The Department has always valued humanity and upheld justice, so it has specifically reported the situation and requested a thorough investigation, and forwarded it to the superior Party Department for prompt investigation to punish negligence and quell public outrage, which would be greatly appreciated." Based on this, it is reasonable to report the situation and request a thorough investigation, and forward it to the Municipal Party Department for investigation. The Department believes that the matter concerns human life and legal principles, so it is not appropriate to remain silent. It has sent personnel to conduct a thorough investigation of the points presented by Ren Xincai, which are indeed true. Yu A'san, a native of Tongzhou, 16 years old, was sent to the hospital by the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's relief section for diagnosis and treatment on January 24, and stayed in the fourth-class No. 1 ward. The doctors who diagnosed and treated him were Doctors Jin and Jiang. Because the doctors saw A'san tearfully complaining that he had been bullied, but he refused to reveal the truth. On February 18, a tea attendant saw A'san hanging himself in the toilet. He quickly persuaded him and inquired about the details, and he said that he had been sodomized by a patient in the same room (name temporarily kept secret). After reporting to the director, the person fled. A'san was transferred to the third-class ward, and he stopped eating. After two days, he suddenly had abdominal pain and vomiting, gradually became unconscious, and died three days later due to heart failure. Based on this, Yu A'san died of shame and refused food after being sodomized, which is not a false statement. The hospital director, Zhou Chuliang, bearing the important responsibility of hospital director, failed to prevent it beforehand, and only knew how to cover up the stain and hastily bury the body afterward, without reporting the person who committed the act to the authorities for investigation. This is indeed poor management and disregard for human life. It is reasonable to report the situation to your commission for a thorough investigation, and request the Municipal Government to remove the hospital director to punish negligence and value humanity, which would be greatly appreciated. Respectfully submitted to the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipality of the Chinese Kuomintang."

Red Pills

The detectives immediately detained the two women and searched them thoroughly. What they had hidden was red pills and manufacturing equipment, including 36,000 red pills seized, packed in several bags, as well as a pill-making rolling board, medicinal materials, a sieve, a seal, bags for holding pills, etc. They were taken to the police station. When questioned, the two women said, "Our family specializes in manufacturing, working at night. The owner is Zhou Rongchuan from Chaozhou, living at No. 1, Shunqing Lane, Bair Road." The detectives went to Shunqing Lane and arrested Zhou. In his room, several bags of sample red pills, about several thousand pills, were found inside a porcelain hollow Maitreya Buddha on the dresser. They were immediately taken to the police station. It was found that Zhou Rongchuan was also known as Zhou Jinhai. In July of the year before last, he was arrested for private possession of drugs, and the court sentenced him to a fine of 300 yuan. Last June, he was arrested again for opening a red pill hall, and the court sentenced him to three months in prison. It is clear that he specializes in running a red pill business. He was taken into custody together. Yesterday, he was also sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Local Court. Yao Zhaodi, the police station's lawyer, explained the case, briefly stating that the police station still needs to conduct a detailed investigation of this case, requesting that the defendants be detained temporarily and the case be investigated in seven days, requesting interrogation. The court ordered that the interrogation be rescheduled to March

28, and the defendants were returned to custody.

White Pills

These pills are also known as "Quick, Quick," because they are more convenient to take than red pills. He was taken back to the police station. Under interrogation, it was learned that its manufacturing facility was located on the third floor of the Dashengchang Butcher Shop at No. 117, Ximen Road, in the French Concession. They immediately joined forces with detectives from the French Police Department and went to arrest a man named Li Zhengxiang from Wuxi, seizing a large number of machines, raw materials, and smoking paraphernalia for manufacturing white pills. After Judge Feng questioned the two defendants, Xu and Li, he ordered them to be returned to custody and the interrogation to be rescheduled.

Complicated and Fragmented Inside Story of the Qinghefang Assassination Case 162

The Murderer, Chen A'si, Claims the Deceased Framed Him and Sent Him to Prison

And Introduced His Wife to Commit Adultery and Remarry

It has already been reported in this newspaper that on the 15th of this month, at half-past twelve midnight, a Suzhou man named Lu A'san was assassinated at the back gate of No. 602 Qinghefang, Guangdong Road. The case has now been investigated by Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, Detective Song Bingzheng, and Investigator Liu Zhaonian of the General Investigation Department of the General Inspectorate. The murderer's name is Chen A'si, also known as Shen A'si, from Yangzhou, currently hiding at No. 7, Lane 38, Rue Laguerre in the French Concession. They immediately led Detectives Zhang Hongyun and Bao Lisheng to the address, arrested Chen, and confiscated six shell casings, taking them back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were handed over to the First Special District Court's First Criminal Division. Police lawyer Li Zhishan stated that the deceased and his wife, Wang A'gui, went to the home of a woman named Chen Lao'er at No. 602 Qinghefang on the 15th. At the time of the incident, when the deceased and his wife went downstairs to urinate at the back gate, the defendant approached and fired several shots before fleeing. Police detectives rushed to the scene, but the defendant had already escaped. However, the deceased was still conscious and identified Chen A'si as the shooter. After the police investigated and learned his address, they arrested him. According to the defendant's confession, the deceased had previously invited him to rob opium at Xinzha Road, but the deceased reported him to the police, leading to his arrest and conviction. The deceased also seduced his wife and married her off to a rogue named Wu Jinbiao in the French Concession. After the defendant was released from prison, he negotiated with the deceased but was suspected of having an affair with Wang A'gui, who wanted to kill the defendant. Therefore, he struck first and killed the deceased. He stated that he had discarded the pistol in the river. Presiding Judge Feng Shide reviewed the confession and ordered the case to be adjourned for further questioning. Wang A'gui testified that the defendant indeed killed the deceased, but the reason was mainly due to the failure to borrow money and his attempt to have her elope with him, which led to her husband's severe reprimand. When questioned, the defendant Chen A'si admitted to killing Lu A'san but completely denied the two points mentioned by Wang A'gui. He claimed that the deceased not only lured him into theft and then reported him to the police but also introduced his wife to commit adultery. He did not hold a grudge but was falsely accused of having an affair with Wang A'gui and was threatened with death, so he killed him. He stated that he had discarded the pistol in the river. Judge Feng Shide reviewed the confession and ordered the case to be adjourned for further questioning.

A Large Gambling Den Was Cracked Down in Jinglinlu 163

An Italian National Was in Charge

The Poker Game Was Different From Other Gambling Methods

—Eight Men and Women Were Arrested One After Another—

After Deputy Chief Detective Zhu Jihuang of the Hongkou Police Department learned that a person named Boni Asi was running a gambling establishment in the Jinglinlu No. 2 Apartment, he disguised himself as a gambler and entered. He found that the scale was quite large and the stakes were high. He immediately exchanged four marked ten-yuan banknotes from the Bank of Communications for chips and joined the game. The game was poker, but the rules were different from those outside. Before long, he lost all his chips and left. He then reported to the Italian Consulate and obtained a search warrant. At 1:45 AM the day before yesterday, he executed the warrant, arresting the owner, the Italian Boni Asi; a host, the Russian Qin Sbao; a chip changer, the Greek Mike Leisi; a boss, the Russian Funa Zefu; and gamblers, the Russian Tang Gen, the Brazilian Kala Si, La Liushi, and a Cantonese woman Chen Ailian, totaling eight people. Except for Boni, who was handed over to the Italian Consulate, the rest were detained. Yesterday morning, they were handed over to the Fifth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu presented the case, stating that the defendant Kala Si jumped out of the window to escape when the police arrived, causing a foot injury. He is now being treated in the hospital and cannot attend court today. When questioned, the defendants admitted to gambling, but Qin, Mai, and Fu denied helping Boni Asi run the gambling den. Judge Deng Baosun reviewed the confession and ordered the verdict to be announced on the morning of the 21st. Tang Gen was released on bail of one hundred yuan, and the rest were remanded in custody.

Mexico Plans to Purchase Chinese Art 164

According to a message released yesterday by the International Trade Bureau, Chinese porcelain, such as teapots, teacups, bowls, vases, and bronze ware, such as new embossed, purple light pots, purple light sets, yellow pots, and tinware, such as candlesticks, incense burners, and other square pieces, as well as round pieces such as teapots, bottles, plates, Fujian lacquerware, and various antique metal artwork, are very popular among foreigners. Exports are not small every year. In recent years, various export merchants in Shanghai have actively improved their products to cater to foreign psychology in order to develop foreign trade. Recently, the Mexican Manier Cogado Company sent a letter to the International Trade Bureau, intending to purchase various Chinese art products and requesting price information. Manufacturers who wish to trade with Mexico can contact the International Trade Bureau to promote their products. The bureau is located on the fourth floor of the Jianghai Customs Building on Sanma Road in this port.

The Shanghai North National Products Exhibition Sends a Telegram to Minister Chen Requesting Him to Hold the Opening Ceremony 165

The Opening Ceremony Will Be Held on the 22nd

Invitations Are Sent to Various Agencies and Organizations to Attend the Ceremony

The Shanghai North National Products Exhibition on Datong Road, Zhabei, this city, was originally scheduled to open today. However, due to delays in the delivery of goods from factories in other ports, a telegram was sent requesting a postponement. After receiving the telegram, the association decided at a representative meeting to postpone the opening by two days to the 22nd. Yesterday, invitations were widely sent to various agencies and organizations to attend the opening ceremony. A telegram was also sent to Minister Chen Gongbo of the Ministry of Industry, requesting him to attend the ceremony to show solemnity. The original telegram stated: "Respected Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry of the Nanjing National Government, dumping of foreign goods, increasing trade deficit year after year, outflow of money, the foundation of the country is in danger. If we do not try to rescue it urgently, the industry and factories will have the danger of stopping work, and the social economy will also show signs of collapse. The association, in view of this, specially initiated the Shanghai North National Products Exhibition, collecting national products for public display, in order to give the Chinese people an opportunity to recognize national products, so as to arouse their concept of enjoying national products. Now the preparations have been completed, and it is scheduled to open at 2 pm on the 22nd of this month. We respectfully invite you to attend and preside over the opening ceremony to show solemnity and encouragement."

Wang Yiting and Others Initiate the Longhua Temple Select the Virtuous to Protect the Dharma Association 166

Since the Buddhist Association appointed Dharma Master Xingkong from the Ten Thousand Buddha Peak of Mount Emei to preside over Longhua Temple, the temple has been renovated and renewed. Now, during the Peach Blossom Festival, Wang Yiting, Huang Fusheng, Guan Jiongzhi, and others who have always believed in Buddhism, intend to initiate a Dharma Protection Association to maintain the Dharma. It is heard that among those who have joined are Shi Shengzhi, Wang Zhixiang, Huang Qinglan, Yang Xingchen, Zhu Shizeng, "Dabei," "Mingdao," "Nanyi," "Dehao," "Rongxu," "Zhenkong," "Huikai," "Huizong," "Kundi," "Yuelai," "Dalin," "Yuanchen," "Yinzong," Bai Zihou, Liao Songbai, Wen Disheng, Wang Shaohu, Li Jingwei, He Huiyin, He Yuquan, Zhu Jinhua, Li Yuangao, Zhang Songling, Zheng Shengzheng, Yao Hui, Song Baoshu, Lin Haishan, Yu Zhiyuan, Yang Huitong, Shen Binhan, Li Bingcheng, Zhong Bolian, Wen Ru, Liu Renhang, Yang Chunkui, Zhang Zhuming, "Jiecheng," Wei Chengshi, Qian Ying, Zhu Shouyan, Ye Erkai, Ma Boshen, Qian Huafu, Xu Chunrong, Zhu Jihua, Li Ming, Jia Dongchu, Chen Wen, "Rigao," "Changan," Ji Zhukang, Qian Qingzheng, Ye Yufu, and more than a hundred others. The Longhua Ancient Temple has a history of more than two thousand years and is a place of observation for China and foreign countries. Now, with the enthusiastic support of all the lay Buddhists and monks, the Dharma will be glorious again, and the scenic spot will be glorious, which can be predicted.

Preparation of the World Guanyin Wan Yuan Association 167

The World Guanyin Wan Yuan Association was initiated and organized by Dr. Liu Renhang and various celebrities in the country. It was first initiated in Yangzhou in the 18th year of the Republic of China, and the capital was the second initiation. In the 19th year, it was established in Shanghai, Nanyang, Singapore, Penang, Yangon, as well as the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River, and various provinces along the Yellow River. The purpose is to eliminate international war and pray for world peace. Now, when the Panchen Lama came south, he learned about the situation of the association and strongly supported it. With the addition of Wang Yiting, Shi Liangcai, Peng Yangguang, and other gentlemen, we strive to expand the organization. The association held its first preparatory meeting at Qiliang Temple yesterday afternoon. More than 30 people, including Qinghai, Liu Renhang, Chao Yi, Yang Xingchen, Puzhao, Chanding, Shi Liangcai (represented by Liu Renhang), Zhu Yuxuan, and Xie Mengfang, attended to discuss all matters. The scope of the association is very wide, and it is actively searching for a suitable venue to proceed. It is heard that the number of people joining is extremely enthusiastic.

National Medical Federation Executive Committee 168

The National Medical Practitioners' Association held its third meeting of the third executive committee yesterday. The committee members present were Chen Fangzhi, Xu Naili, Jiang Zhenxun, Wang Qizhang, Niu Huisheng (represented by Xu), and Yu Yunxiu (represented by Chen). Xu Naili presided.

(A) Reports:

(1) Report on the minutes of the third executive committee meeting of the third session, held on February 4th.

(2) Regarding the Ministry of Interior's approval on January 2nd, Wei Zi No. 7, requesting local health authorities to strictly enforce the Midwives Regulations and train old-style midwives, it was reported that "The submitted matters have merit. Regarding the banning and training of old-style midwives, the former Ministry of Health had already issued orders to comply. In addition to further requesting the provincial and municipal governments to instruct local health authorities to strictly enforce the Midwives Regulations and to strictly implement the previous orders and the Regulations for the Management of Midwives, it is hereby approved for your information."

(3) The Hankou Medical Association sent a letter requesting the transfer to the Ministry of Interior to explicitly order the Hankou Municipal Government to cancel the "Hankou Municipal Government's mandatory registration of clinics." The case had been submitted by the Association to the Ministry of Interior's Health Department on February 17th, requesting that the Hankou Municipal Government be ordered to cancel it. The department's reply was as follows.

(4) An item was received on March 14th from the Ministry of Interior's Health Department, approval No. 49, requesting the submission and order to the Hankou Municipal Government to abolish the "Provisional Regulations for Clinic Registration." "It has been noted that the Ministry has already instructed the Hubei Provincial Department of Civil Affairs to handle the matter. Please be informed."

(B) Discussions:

(1) The Hangzhou Medical Association sent a letter stating that Qiu Boxun, a member of the Association, was falsely accused of professional negligence due to the death of Wang Xifei. They requested a public evaluation on academic grounds to clear his name, and requested a further review. "Decision": Liu Yixiang, Zhou Jingwen, Chen Fangzhi, Yu Lin, and Luo Chuanrong, five experts, were nominated to review the case, convened by Chen Fangzhi. A letter should be sent to the Hangzhou Medical and Pharmaceutical Association to collect detailed materials for reference.

(2) The Hangzhou Medical and Pharmaceutical Association requested that the Judicial Yuan issue a general order to all local courts to handle medical and pharmaceutical cases with caution. In addition to forensic doctors and forensic chemists, medical and pharmaceutical experts should be employed as much as possible to participate in investigations or juries, and scientific verification and proof should be carried out to avoid errors and ensure fairness. "Decision": Approved.

(3) The Chinese Medical Association will hold its second general meeting after the merger in Nanjing from March 31st to April 7th. A letter was sent to the Association requesting it to send representatives to participate. "Decision": Chu Minyi, Hu Ding'an, Jin Mingyu, and Chen Wenda were nominated as representatives of the Association to participate, and Wang Qizhang was nominated to draft a congratulatory speech.

(4) Xu Xucai of Kunshan sent a letter requesting answers to five medical questions. "Decision": The Association has a long-standing policy of not answering inquiries entrusted in a personal capacity. A letter should be sent to explain this.

(5) Liu Baiping of Guangdong sent a letter requesting assistance in applying for registration. "Decision": Upon investigation, Mr. Liu is not a member of the Association. He should be informed to directly submit his application to the competent authority.

(6) Discussion on whether to change the publication schedule of the Association's quarterly journal, "Medical Affairs Collection." "Decision": Starting this year, the publication will be changed to January, April, July, and October. Each period will be one volume, and starting next year, it will be Volume 7. The original issue number must still be indicated in each issue.

(7) The Zhangjiakou Medical Association of Chahar Province applied for membership. "Decision": A letter should be sent requesting them to send the resumes of the members, and the matter will be submitted for review at the next routine meeting.

Renewal of Business Licenses for Restaurants in the Urban Area 169

—Extended to the End of March—

The validity period of business licenses for restaurants in this city is limited to one year. According to regulations, they must report to the Municipal Health Bureau for registration and renew their licenses before March 15th of the following year. Failure to do so will result in penalties according to regulations. March 15th of this year has already passed the deadline for license renewal. However, because the Health Bureau relocated to its new building in the Central District of the city before the New Year, some restaurants may not be aware of the Health Bureau's new address. Therefore, while many restaurants have renewed their licenses according to regulations, a few restaurants have not yet reported for renewal. The Municipal Health Bureau, recognizing that there is a legitimate reason for this, has reportedly extended the renewal period to the end of March. Failure to renew the license by the deadline will result in penalties according to regulations, without leniency.

Grand Spring Banquet of China-America Tobacco Company 170

Jing Yimeng, the General Manager of China-America Tobacco Company, along with Xie Li Wang Yongchang, Yu Zhong'e, and Han Xushan, and Song Yincun, District Chiefs of Jiangsu Province, hosted a banquet at the Zhimei Restaurant yesterday, inviting managers from Wing On, Sincere, The Sun Sun, Lihua, China National Goods Company, and major tobacco companies. More than 500 representatives attended, including Sheng Changyong's Yu Aiyu, Qian Tai Xin's Zhong Juncai, and He Kang's Xu Xisheng. During the banquet, each person was presented with 100 sticks of the company's new high-quality ginseng brand cigarettes. After trying them, the rich flavor was greatly praised. The banquet ended in joy at 10 o'clock. It is said that each pack of cigarettes is sold for only 15 copper coins and sales have already begun today.

Two People Commit Suicide in Hotels 171

Liu Huiqing, a 33-year-old from Shandong, checked into the Baohe Hotel on Xieqiao Road in Nanshi around 5 p.m. the day before yesterday. After paying the room fee, he closed the door and went to sleep. At 11 a.m. yesterday, the bellboy heard groaning sounds from the room and suspected something was wrong. He pried open the door and saw Liu lying stiffly on the bed with a pale face. He had taken poison. The bellboy reported to the front desk, and Liu was rushed to Renji Hospital. He died despite efforts to save him.

At the Danghu Hotel on Shanxi Road in the Public Concession, a traveler who claimed to be Wu Shunxian, 20 years old, checked into room 22 the night before last. For unknown reasons, Wu Shunxian suddenly had thoughts of death and swallowed raw opium behind people's backs to commit suicide. It was not until around 10 a.m. yesterday that the bellboy discovered him. He reported to the front desk, who then reported to the police. Detective No. 116 was dispatched to investigate. Shunxian was rushed to Renji Hospital, but because he had ingested a large amount of poison, he died before treatment could be administered. He was sent to the coroner's office for examination. According to the reporter's investigation, the deceased's real name was Tang Yuanhong, from Ningbo.

Rickshaw Pullers Petition the Municipal Council 172

Rickshaw Committee to Discuss Tomorrow

Thousands of rickshaw pullers in the city jointly submitted a petition to the Municipal Council yesterday, expressing their opposition to the Rickshaw Committee's recent proposals and seeking to reduce the heavy rickshaw rental fee from 14 cents to 8 cents small coin. The Municipal Council has taken the petition seriously and has scheduled a joint meeting of the Rickshaw Committee and the Police Committee for Wednesday afternoon to discuss the matter.

Public Concession Health Conditions for February 173

Good Health Conditions Last Month

The Head of the Municipal Council Health Department reports for February: The health conditions within the concession were quite good this month. Smallpox was quite prevalent for several weeks, but the public need not panic excessively if they utilize the Health Department's vaccination facilities. Scarlet fever and influenza were also quite prevalent. Regarding the former, school children should immediately seek medical attention if they feel discomfort in their throat. The latter should also not be neglected, as delays can harm both the individual and society. One case of leprosy was discovered in the prison hospital. The patient was a Cantonese man, 23 years old. It is unknown where he contracted the disease. Measles cases are currently increasing. Five cases of meningitis were discovered, four of whom were Chinese. Typhoid fever has decreased among both Chinese and foreigners. The Health Department administered vaccinations. The motor vehicle team administered 10,971 vaccinations, and the branch offices administered 5,594 vaccinations. Due to the cold weather and the Spring Festival, the public did not pay sufficient attention to this. Regarding vital statistics, the reported birth rate for foreigners this month was 16.07 per thousand. The reported birth rate for Chinese was only nine per ten thousand, likely representing only a small fraction of the total. The mortality rate was 11.8 for foreigners and 14.6 for Chinese, both lower than usual. The total number of Chinese deaths was 1,327, including 651 unclaimed corpses found on the east and west borders. The pathological laboratory performed 1,896 chemical tests, and the chemical laboratory performed 535 analyses. The rabies clinic treated 44 people, five of whom were from outside the city. Thirty-six people were advised to receive treatment, and three people did not complete their treatment. The newly built rabies observation room is now in use and is quite satisfactory. Both the foreign and Chinese isolation hospitals were busy due to smallpox and scarlet fever. Four foreigners and twenty-six Chinese were admitted to the hospital with diphtheria. The Chinese section of the Police Hospital had 1,683 outpatient visits, 151 inpatients, and two deaths. The Indian section was quite quiet. The Walderloo Road Prison Hospital had 835 admissions and 19 deaths, 11 of whom had tuberculosis. The Mental Hospital can accommodate severe cases, but there are still no vacancies for ordinary cases. Milk production has decreased slightly. Samples were subjected to bacterial tests and all passed. However, four samples failed the chemical test at grade B and one at grade A. The illegal sale of milk by unlicensed Indians has been investigated again. The number of slaughtered pigs has decreased due to the Spring Festival, exceeding the record. Other slaughter numbers have decreased. Over 30,000 pounds of substandard meat were disposed of. The output of by-products has increased. The vegetable market business is very prosperous, and inspections and calibration of weights and measures are still carried out on time. Bakeries are often inspected in the early morning due to the limited amount of night work. Food stores have been inspected, and items that do not comply with regulations have been warned or prosecuted separately.

To prevent mosquitoes, many ditches and rivers have been cleaned. Unregistered sheds have been found in the eastern and western districts, and the Public Works Department has been notified to remove them.

Public Concession Police Affairs for February 174

727 Released Under Amnesty, Rearrested for New Cases The Head of the Municipal Council Police Department reports for February: There were 1,029 reported criminal cases this month, 233 fewer than in January and 371 fewer than in the same month last year. A total of 1,746 criminals were captured, more than in the previous month and the same month last year. In addition, 113 people were arrested for old cases, and 42 people were arrested on behalf of other government agencies. Five murder cases were reported this month and two attempted murder cases. There were 49 armed robbery cases, five fewer than last month. The reported value of stolen property was $264,967.43, of which $24,894.28 was recovered. Twenty-eight criminals were released under the amnesty law, including six repeat offenders, four with old cases, and eighteen first-time offenders. In total, 2,628 people have been released under the amnesty, of whom 727 have been rearrested for new cases. Five people were arrested for promoting communism, one of whom has been transferred to the Chinese authorities. The remaining four were still pending trial at the end of the month. Twenty-four residences were searched and 3,500 pieces of propaganda were seized, including some in English intended for distribution to British and American troops. The rest were mostly anniversary documents. There were seven strikes in the concession this month, affecting 3,126 workers and resulting in 2,495 lost workdays. Sixty-five feature films and 128 short films were inspected. Thirty-five feature films were approved, 24 were ordered to be revised, and four were rejected. The remaining two were pending. 122 short films were approved, four were ordered to be revised, and two were under consideration at the end of the month. There were 3,747 traffic violations, of which 445 were prosecuted (29 foreigners and 416 Chinese). The rest were warned. There were 924 accident cases, with 262 injuries and 10 deaths. Accidents involving bicycles occurred 178 times. 1,318 rickshaw pullers were prosecuted for violations in the Central and Laoza districts.

Dismissal of Appeal in the Tang Jiapeng Assassination Case Concluding Arguments 175

The assassination of Tang Jiapeng, manager of the Rongji amusement park at the Great World, last summer, resulted in the arrest of the perpetrators Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Xiaosizi by the French Concession police. A pistol used by Zhao to kill Tang was also retrieved. After investigation and trial by the Second Special District Court, Zhao was sentenced to life imprisonment and Zhang to 20 years imprisonment. Because both convicts appealed to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, the High Court opened a hearing some time ago and announced its conclusion, scheduling a date for sentencing, as reported previously. It has been learned that Presiding Judge Guo Dezhang, after reviewing the entire case file, found that there were still points of doubt in the case that needed to be thoroughly examined in order to avoid wrongful conviction. Therefore, yesterday, he convened a hearing and announced the dismissal of the concluding arguments before the appellants arrived in court, and scheduled a date to reopen the arguments.

The 22nd Branch of the Shanghai First Special District Citizen's Federation, since its preparation by Wang Honghui and others, has completed all procedures. Yesterday afternoon, a founding meeting was held at No. 7 Hongde Lane, Zhejiang Road. Representatives Zhao Erchang from the Municipal Party Department, Zhang Xianfang from the Municipal Federation, guest Liu Zhongying, and more than 30 members attended. Dong Yunlong, Xue Guangqian, and Tang Yuanji were elected as alternates. After the election, the first executive committee meeting was held and adjourned at 5 p.m.

Gu Zhuxuan, owner of the Tianchan Stage, married his daughter yesterday. The shop was set up in the Yangbu Public Office, with thousands of guests and more than ten thousand gifts received. The Pingju opera performance continued until midnight, truly a grand occasion for the time.

Death of Zhou Zhen, Director of the Baoshan County Security Corps 178

Zhou Zhen, currently the Deputy Commander of the Baoshan County Security Corps Headquarters, courtesy name Shufan, was from Baoshan. He served as the Director of the Security Corps of the County Government and a member of the Baoshan County Party Committee. He was known for his intelligence, competence, hard work, and dedication. He had been running around for the revolution and serving the community for many years, with significant achievements. Unfortunately, he passed away permanently at 3 p.m. on March 17th, and those who knew him and those who didn't deeply mourned his passing.

Medical and Pharmaceutical News 179

Hualong Chinese Medicine Hospital with Complete Facilities The Hualong Chinese Medicine Hospital, located at the intersection of Beller Road and Huageguo Road in the French Concession, was founded by the famous Shanghai doctor, Mr. Ding Jiwan. In the past four years, it has achieved remarkable results. The number of dangerous illnesses that have been cured is countless. The hospital has a quiet location, spacious rooms, and ample air. Nurses are on duty day and night, and doctors are stationed in the hospital. Special contracted doctors include Mr. Xia Yingtang, Wang Zhongqi, Zhu Nanshan, and Zhu Ziyun. When there are difficult and dangerous illnesses, they will consult together. If patients wish to be hospitalized, they can call 84729, and the hospital will send a patient car to pick them up. Outpatient consultations are from 9 a.m. to 3 p.m. The price for a regular consultation is 20 cents small coin, and a special consultation is $1.20. Medicine is provided to the indigent. The hospital is the only one in Chinese medicine that can be called complete, so we are happy to introduce it.

Dr. Song Daren Cures Threatened Abortion Mrs. Zhou Luqiu, manager of the Fuli Yuan Leather Goods Store on Henan Road, was more than four months pregnant and experiencing prolonged bleeding, abdominal pain, headaches, lower back pain, foot swelling, poor appetite, fatigue, and weakness. More than ten specialists in gynecology, both Chinese and Western doctors, were hired to diagnose and treat her, costing thousands of dollars, but the symptoms worsened. Fortunately, Dr. Song, the director of the World Hospital across from the Nanjing Grand Theater, treated her for several days, and she saw results. Her body grew stronger day by day. Now, because she has given birth to a son, her family is overjoyed and has specially made a large plaque with the inscription "Gynecological Master" to give to Dr. Song Daren as a memorial.

City News 180

New Offering of Domestic Glass Cups The Zhongshan Glass Factory, in view of the fact that ladies and gentlemen in society often suffer from not being able to buy domestic, high-quality, and inexpensive hot water cups, which has led to the market being flooded with foreign goods, has specially hired expert technicians to painstakingly research and produce various kinds of Labor Brand hot water cups. The styles are ingenious and durable. It is said that the cups are guaranteed not to explode at a high temperature of 140 degrees Celsius. If the above situation occurs, you can bring the original cup to Zhongshan Glass Factory at No. 980 Kangqu Road, Dapulu Road, Nanshi, or to the factory's distribution office at No. 419 Mingzhu Street, Fuyou Road, inside the old North Gate, to exchange it for a new cup. Among the various colors, the electro-optic cup is the most exquisite. This cup is not only the best among domestic hot water cups, but also no less excellent than imported products. This is indeed good news in the voice of promoting domestic goods. The factory also manufactures various other glass materials and utensils, and the prices are very cheap.

Grand Auction at the Daxiang Silk and Satin Store The Daxiang Silk and Satin Store on Sanma Road and Shilu Road in this city is undergoing a reorganization into a national goods company and urgently needs to hand over the store's base. It began a large-scale auction of its inventory yesterday. Around 9 a.m., a large number of customers had gathered at the corner of Fujian Road, because all sectors of society know that the store selects its goods carefully. Now, because of the reorganization auction, the goods are of good quality and low price, which is extraordinary. By 10 a.m., the prices of all goods were truly low and cheap, such as line spring trousers material sold for only one yuan per piece. The total sales for the entire day amounted to more than 17,000 yuan. In this time of social recession, such a grand occasion is truly unprecedented.

Daxing Dyeing and Weaving Factory Expands The Daxing Dyeing and Weaving Factory on Roushenfu Road in the French Concession has been established for many years, specializing in dyeing Indigo and various colors of domestic fabrics. The colors are long-lasting and do not fade. Recently, because most school uniforms use these fabrics, the factory has greatly expanded to meet demand. Its product trademarks include the Three Stars picture and Zhao Zilong and other varieties.
