Reading News, First Issue

Table of Contents 185

Seven Items of Small News and a Public Letter

Compiled by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shen Bao Circulation Library

A Word from Xiaobian: It has been two and a half months since the Shen Bao Circulation Library established the Reading Guidance service. During these two months, our small endeavor has garnered attention from some individuals in the society. We have received 500 letters from readers discussing academic matters, and over 200 people have formally applied to register as regular researchers of this department. The influence of the Reading Q&A section has been even more extensive, as we can see from the letters we receive from other locations. Geographically, we have received letters from readers in all provinces of China, except for Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, and Guizhou, wherever the Shen Bao newspaper reaches. They all unanimously approve of our work and enthusiastically request to join the Reading Guidance service, jointly studying practical knowledge needed by everyone. According to the Shen Bao's circulation figures, roughly at least one-third or more of the readers read the Reading Q&A section (over 50,000 people). Among them, the majority not only enjoy reading the "Reading Q&A," but also repeatedly write to inquire about more news regarding our work. They want to know everything about the entire "Reading Guidance" operation.

To reduce the trouble of individually replying to readers from other locations, and to further maintain a spiritual connection among registered readers, we urgently need to publish a periodical as a means of spiritual communication. Therefore, given the limited talent and financial resources of this department at present, we are launching "Reading News" in advance. It will be published every Tuesday, continuing to be printed in the original location of the "Reading Q&A" in the Shen Bao, but on the same day, the "Reading Q&A" will be discontinued.

In the future, it will faithfully report all "Reading News" to friends across the country who care about us.

Information: (1) Quick Statistics: (1) The number of readers who have borrowed books from the Shen Bao Circulation Library is approximately 7,000. (2) The current number of active book-borrowing readers is 4,500. (3) The number of people who have joined the Reading Guidance Department is 200. (4) The number of people who have joined the "Reading Q&A" correspondence is 500 (including Shen Bao readers from other locations). (5) The composition of readers who have joined the Reading Guidance: 80% are shop assistants and apprentices, 10% are lower-level freelancers, 3% are students, 3% are workers, and 4% are others. (2) Regular work for registered readers: (1) Assisting readers in formulating personal reading plans. (2) Helping readers solve general reading problems. (3) Helping readers resolve doubts about the meaning of words or sentences in books. (4) Providing readers with more accurate reading methods. (5) Recommending suitable reading materials to readers. (6) Accepting discussions on all personal life issues related to readers and reading. (The above six items have been implemented.) (7) Assisting readers in organizing reading groups when necessary. (8) Conducting individual conversations with readers when necessary. (9) Holding lecture meetings and departmental research meetings when necessary. (10) Checking readers' progress. (The above four items have not yet been implemented.) (3) Regular work for Shen Bao readers from other locations: (1) Making the "Reading Q&A" public to all friends who are interested in engaging in academic discussions with us and who love reading this newspaper. (2) For friends who have a special enthusiasm for the work of this department and request to participate in joint research, we may also make accommodations, permitting them to join if the department believes they are sincere. After a certain period, we may also provide relevant reading materials by mail and allow them to enjoy the general book-borrowing rights of readers who are away from Shanghai. (4) Starting reader talks: For readers who lack written expression skills or whose questions are complex and cannot be answered with brief text, this department will specially arrange for talks at the library. The talk time is scheduled for 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM on Sunday afternoons. However, it is temporarily limited to readers who have joined the research of this department; and they must hold a special appointment letter from this department as an introduction. (5) Establishment of book-borrowing guidance (implemented on April 1): (1) To help book-borrowing readers of this library select reading materials, the library management department has specially established book-borrowing guidance, which is the responsibility of this department. (2) Readers who do not know what reading materials to select may submit a request for book-borrowing guidance to the book-borrowing office of this library. (3) Anyone who decides to study a certain subject but does not know what books to read. (4) Anyone who is studying a specific practical problem and wants to collect information. (6) Publication announcement: Within March, this department will print and publish books: (1) How to learn literature on your own? (2) How to learn social sciences on your own? (3) How to learn English on your own? (7) Readers of this library are welcome to join this department. Details of the joining procedure can be found on page 8 of the library catalog.

Public Letter: (1) To all registered members: (1) Those who have already made reading plans, please immediately follow the plans, select reading materials, and work diligently, and at any time, submit any difficulties to the department, and the department will not be afraid of trouble and will provide explanations. Those who have not made good reading plans, please quickly make them and send them to the library, or come to the library in person to discuss them. (2) Please number your letters yourself, such as "First Communication," "No. ... Communication," for statistical purposes. (3) For all inquiries that are not from books borrowed from this library and that are not available in this library, please send the original book to the library together. A reply will be made within three days and the original book will be returned. (If the original book is indeed of considerable value, this library will naturally purchase it. Readers only need to provide the title, publisher, and price.) (4) For specialized questions, if this department cannot reply immediately, it will reply by letter within half a month; if a correct answer still cannot be found within half a month, it will reply with "I don't know," and will never pretend to know what it does not know, distort explanations, or deceive readers. (5) All letters do not need to use polite language, and each letter should be limited to one central question. If there are many questions, multiple communications can be made, and this department will never find it troublesome. (6) Please report your work progress every month. (7) For any two months without communication to this department or without submitting a work report to this department, this department will immediately cancel the registration and publish the name in this publication; however, this does not apply to cases where the person has declared illness or an accident or is away from Shanghai. (8) Before the Self-Study Series of this department is published, if readers have any questions about self-study of a certain subject, they can submit a request for a face-to-face discussion to this department, and the department will schedule a time for a face-to-face discussion.

Shanghai Has a Uniquely Large Number with Twenty-Five Schools

Because the national vocational schools and above change from time to time, the Ministry of Education, in order to understand the latest national higher education situation, has made a "Distribution Status Table of National Vocational Schools and Above" above February of this year after a long period of investigation, for reference. Age of Students in National Vocational Schools and Above 187

The Ministry of Education has statistically analyzed the age of students in national vocational schools and above (universities, independent colleges, and vocational schools). Students in universities and independent colleges range from sixteen years old and above to thirty years old and above, while vocational schools have students under sixteen years old. The details are listed below.

Universities: According to statistics from universities nationwide (thirteen national, nine provincial, and nineteen private, in total), the number of students by age is as follows: sixteen years old: 12 students; seventeen years old: 105 students; eighteen years old: 418 students; nineteen years old: 1,007 students; twenty years old: 1,895 students; twenty-one years old: 2,433 students; twenty-two years old: 2,905 students; twenty-three years old: 2,734 students; twenty-four years old: 2,141 students; twenty-five years old: 1,499 students; twenty-six years old: 962 students; twenty-seven years old: 555 students; twenty-eight years old: 336 students; twenty-nine years old: 207 students; thirty years old: 99 students; thirty years old and above: 105 students. The total number of students is 17,413.

Independent Colleges: According to statistics from independent colleges nationwide (five national, eleven provincial, and eighteen private, in total), the number of students by age is as follows: sixteen years old: 1 student; seventeen years old: 12 students; eighteen years old: 81 students; nineteen years old: 197 students; twenty years old: 360 students; twenty-one years old: 477 students; twenty-two years old: 515 students; twenty-three years old: 512 students; twenty-four years old: 427 students; twenty-five years old: 329 students; twenty-six years old: 225 students; twenty-seven years old: 146 students; twenty-eight years old: 81 students; twenty-nine years old: 56 students; thirty years old: 46 students; thirty years old and above: 66 students. The total number of students is 3,531.

Jiangda Basketball Game Yesterday 199

Fudan Defeats Guanghua

Jinan Loses to Zhongda

Jinling Decisively Beats Chizhi

—Women's Jinan Defeats Zhongda—

A Jiangda basketball game was held in Shanghai yesterday. Fudan decisively defeated Guanghua, with a final score of 57 to 24.

Situation of the Game in Nanjing Last Night

(Nanjing, 19th) In the Jiangda Basketball Championship, Central University played against Jinan in both the men's and women's divisions last night. The games were held at Zhongda. At 7:30 PM, the women's game began. Jinan's team was strong. Liu Mali was tall and powerful, while Zhongda's passing was disorganized. Jinan was much better. In the first half, Jinan took the lead with a score of 15 to 4. In the second half, they scored 13 to 2. As a result, Jinan decisively defeated Central University with a score of 28 to 6. At 8:30 PM, the men's game began. The strengths of both sides were evenly matched, and the battle was fierce. The scores fluctuated constantly, with moments of great excitement. In the first half, Central University took the lead with a score of 20 to 14. In the second half, Jinan adjusted its strategy and launched a strong counterattack, resulting in a score of 9 to 13 in the second half. As a result, Jinan narrowly lost by two points, with a final score of 29 to 27. In the game between Jinling and Chizhi, held at Zhongda on the 19th, Jinling scored 36 to 12 in the first half and 27 to 18 in the second half. As a result, Jinling decisively defeated Chizhi with a score of 63 to 30.

Final Triangle Match of the International Women's Basketball Championship 201

China Defeats the United States and Gains the Right to the Final

China's Offense Surges in the Second Half, Leading to the Collapse of the United States' Defense

As a Result, China Wins 38 to 29

—China and Britain to Compete for the Championship Tomorrow Night

In the final triangle match of the International Women's Basketball Championship, China defeated the United States in the preliminary round last night with a score of 38 to 29, eliminating the United States and winning the right to compete against Britain in the final. The final between China and Britain will be held tomorrow night to determine the championship winner.

Subordinate to Others

At the start of the game, the United States' momentum was strong. Although Yang Sen made consecutive free throws, Bennett responded in kind. With the collaboration of Bowsake and Bennett, the United States took the lead with a score of 7 to 2. They were dominant and seemed invincible. Although Yang Sen narrowed the gap by two points, the United States still won the first quarter with a score of 9 to 6, then 11 to 6. Starting from the second quarter, China remained subordinate to others. At 15 to 9, China was trailing by six points, and the situation was precarious and worrying. Pan Meng deployed Chen Rongming and Chen Jucai, and with the combined efforts of Chen and Pan, the score was narrowed to 16 to 13, trailing by only three points. The first half ended temporarily.

Military Might Greatly Enhanced

In the second half, Chen Rongming was deployed again, and China's military might suddenly surged. With overwhelming momentum, they shattered the United States' defense, causing them to be unable to defend on all fronts. Chen Rongming and Yang Sen displayed their prowess, scoring twelve points in a row, reversing the situation and taking the lead with a score of 25 to 16, overwhelming the United States. From then on, everything went smoothly. The United States' strength was depleted. In the third quarter, the score was 30 to 19, with China leading by eleven points. The outcome of the game was largely determined. In the final quarter, the United States was busy adjusting its lineup but was unable to recover. The final score was 38 to 29, with China winning the right to the final.

Changes to the 1933-1934 Women's Basketball Rules 202

Announced by the National Sports Association

In Chapter 4, Section C, Article 1, add the following sentence to the note: If the ball is thrown up due to an unstable catch, but its height does not exceed the player's head, it shall not be considered an "illegal scoop."

In Chapter 4, Section C, Article 2, delete the sentence: "When dribbling, the height of the ball bouncing up must be at least equal to the knee of the dribbler."

Add Section D to Chapter 4: Guarding, in its entirety, as follows:

Guarding is an important technique in defense, used to prevent an opponent who has already obtained the ball. When guarding, one arm or both arms can be extended on any plane, but must not touch the ball or the opponent's body. When guarding in a corner of the court, only one arm can be used.

In theory, basketball is a non-contact game, but in reality, because players are running quickly within a limited area, it is impossible to completely avoid physical contact. Such contact should not be penalized if there is no violent behavior. If one unintentionally touches the ball in the opponent's hand or the opponent's body, and immediately releases it, it is also not necessary to penalize.

Revise Article 2 of Chapter 6 in its entirety, as follows:

If the ball goes out of bounds during the game, the player from the team that did not cause the ball to go out of bounds should throw or pass the ball from outside the boundary line at the point where the ball went out of bounds to a player inside the boundary. If the referee or inspector discovers an error, they should immediately correct it, handing the ball to the player with the right to throw the ball into the court. If there is a delay in throwing the ball in after the ball goes out of bounds, it should be considered as "delaying" the game.

Revise the note to Article 2 of Chapter 6 in its entirety, as follows:

If there is not enough space outside the line, players on both sides, except for the thrower, must not approach within three feet of the boundary line. This three-foot distance refers to the entire body of the ball, including the arm.

It would be best to add a thin line three feet inside the boundary line as a standard.

Add the following sentence to Article 1 of Chapter 10, Section A:

If the two teams do not agree on the method of serving, each half can use a different method.

Revise Chapter 10, Section C, Article 2, Item A, (1), as follows:

(1) The players jumping at center court, 1. (Three-zone system) The two team centers should stand with both feet in their own half-circle at center court (the half-circle closer to the opponent's basket). 2. (Two-zone system) The two team centers should stand with both feet in their own half-circle at center court (the half-circle closer to their own basket).

Other players can stand at any location within their own zone, but must not obstruct the actions of the referee, inspector, or centers.

Add Section C to Article 2 of Chapter 11, in its entirety, as follows:

Throwing the ball into the basket after the center circle serve without at least two passes.

The National Sports Community Should Read the Diligent Sports Monthly 205

Introducing the Latest Sports Knowledge

Instructing Various Sports Methods

In recent years, all levels of society in our country have been vigorously promoting sports. However, there is a lack of sports publications to convey new sports knowledge and modern sports techniques. The Qin Fen Bookstore on Laozhou Father Road in Shanghai, recognizing this, has specially invited national sports experts to publish over a hundred kinds of "Sports Series" books, and also publishes the "Diligent Sports Monthly." It has been published on the tenth of every month since Double Ten Day last year, and has now reached its sixth issue. Special issues on the National Games, elementary school sports, and middle school sports have been published. Sports experts Wu Yunrui, Shen Siliang, Hao Gengsheng, Cheng Dengke, Wu Zheng, Wu Bangwei, Jiang Xiangqing, Shang Rumei, Chen Baiqing, Liu Xuesong, Wang Fudan, Wu Tunan, Chen Kuisheng, Wang Jianwu, and others have all contributed articles. The monthly introduces the latest sports knowledge from around the world, provides teaching materials for primary and secondary school teachers, discusses sports administration issues, instructs on exercise methods, details sports news from China and abroad, and includes a readers' forum. Anyone who reads the monthly can submit articles, regardless of length. In addition to text, the monthly includes a pictorial, publishing photos of sports activities from various places, which is quite interesting. All national sports teachers, athletes, school libraries, and sports enthusiasts should have a copy. The monthly has now become popular throughout the country and is a "steel army" among Chinese magazines. To achieve wider circulation, each issue is sold for only two jiao, and a full year of twelve issues is priced at two yuan. Domestic postage is free, and international postage is an additional one yuan and eight jiao.

Spring and Autumn

On Orchids 212

— Nineteen

Every early spring, especially at the beginning of the year, busy places in Suzhou, Shanghai, and Hangzhou are often filled with people selling orchids. They place bundles of orchids in baskets or arrange them along the roadside, waiting for buyers. These orchid sellers mostly come from Xiaoshan in Zhejiang. They travel to the docks and catch the New Year, simply hoping to make a living. Their lives are quite pitiful. Speaking of orchids, they have been cherished, appreciated, and valued by gentlemen and ladies since ancient times. Confucius was one who cherished orchids. For them, he composed the "Yi Lan Cao." The qin score says: "Confucius, returning to Lu from Wei, saw fragrant orchids growing alone in a secluded valley. He sighed, 'Orchids should be the fragrance of kings, but now they grow alone, associating with common weeds!' He stopped his carriage and played the qin. He lamented his ill-fated time, expressing his feelings through the fragrant orchids." Also, Ling Jun used "fragrant grasses and beautiful women" as metaphors. These are clear evidence. The "Zhen Wei" chapter in the Book of Songs says: "The Zhen and Wei rivers flow broadly, men and women hold orchids." It is said that jian means orchids. Imagine, beside the Zhen and Wei rivers, there are clouds of men and women, holding fragrant orchids in their hands. Common flowers would truly be ashamed in comparison. This is ironclad proof that orchids were loved and appreciated by the ancients. Sworn brotherhood is called "righteous alliance of golden orchids." This is based on the Book of Changes: "When two people are of one heart, their strength can break metal; the words of those of one heart are as fragrant as orchids." Liu Bei, Guan Yu, and Zhang Fei formed a brotherhood in Taoyuan, creating a tripartite division of the empire. Which of the heroes on Liangshan Marsh did not go through fire and water, loyal to Song Jiang? All were influenced by the Book of Changes. Although social customs are not as good as in ancient times, there are still many who become enemies the evening after swearing brotherhood in the morning. However, at the beginning of their alliance, did they not hope to be as strong as metal and as fragrant as orchids for the rest of their lives? This is clear evidence that orchids are valued by people.

Today, people prefer novelty and difference. Chrysanthemums, once known for their "reclusive interest," have suffered misfortune, being tied into various shapes by people to cater to vulgar tastes. Fortunately, people still cannot tie up and play with orchids. Although there are exhibitions and gatherings, they are still elegant affairs and not enough to disgrace the orchids. However, according to reports, the puppet state has taken the orchid as its national flower. The reason given is to signify the meaning of forging a lasting "orchid alliance" with Japan. This truly disgraces the orchids. Seeing this, those with a sense of patriotism will probably sing "Nian Jia Shan Po" over and over again. However, if we do not avenge this strange shame, how can we face this "fragrance of kings"? Please, all above and below the nation, think carefully about this.

Taking an X-ray 213

— Shouzi

Recently, a group of people in Shanghai launched a so-called "TB Prevention Conference." The other day, a certain hospital published its TB prevention opinions, saying that TB is most difficult to detect and treat, so it is best to get an X-ray as soon as one has a respiratory illness, so that it can be determined early whether there is lung disease and treated quickly. This sounds very right. However, to whom are these words addressed? If they are addressed to the rich, that is not a problem. If they are addressed to the general public, that is somewhat of a problem.

It is right to take an X-ray for lung disease. However, how to get everyone to take an X-ray is a matter of debate. We know that those who get lung disease the most are those who are malnourished, overworked, live and eat in unsanitary conditions, have difficulty breathing fresh air, and live in great instability. These people are precisely the world's only poor people. The poor are most prone to illness, the poor are most prone to lung disease (referring to urban poor, especially in Shanghai), and the poor are least likely to treat lung disease. The rich can stay in the hospital to recuperate when they are sick, or they can go to Lushan or Moganshan. But what about the poor? To eat and clothe themselves, no matter how sick they are, they cannot but continue their cattle-and-horse-like work for a living. Let alone recuperation, even taking medicine is probably difficult. Please tell me, in this situation, how can you tell the poor how to see a doctor, how to treat lung disease? As soon as you have a respiratory illness, you should immediately take an X-ray. The words are right, but the actual price of taking an X-ray is 15 yuan, at least more than 10 yuan. Please tell me, who can afford to take it? If all the people who get lung disease are rich, then everything is no problem, and there is no need to promote TB prevention. The rich will naturally go to the hospital to ask for advice. But unfortunately, the people who get lung disease are mostly poor. Please tell me, how can this "TB" be "prevented"? If taking an X-ray can be like the free anti-epidemic shots in the hot weather, with cars sent out to give free shots along the streets, that would still have some "TB prevention" effect (but how to treat it after taking it is still a problem). Otherwise, the so-called "TB prevention" is probably just empty talk?

Don't think I'm talking nonsense. I have a friend who has a very serious lung disease, but because of money problems, he has to leave it untreated. He is not considered very poor, but he cannot afford the 30 yuan per month for a third-class ward (he has to stay for at least one year), not to mention anything else. This is a factual issue. If the problem of money is not solved, any "TB prevention" or "no TB prevention" is empty!

— Yuanbai

We need brave warriors, and we also need kind nannies. If there is both the bravery of a warrior and the kindness of a nanny, that is the savior of our nation.

"Conscience" has become a past term in this era. If we use a new tone, it should be the so-called "reason"!

Hypocritical people always stand in front enjoying happiness, and upright people always fall behind suffering. This tells us that now is a world without right and wrong.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 215

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Six

Generously Baring Their Hearts, Forgetting Their Families to Serve the Nation

Sadly Gazing into the Mirror, Sighing for Those I Miss

The common people here returned home, but the situation for the garrison troops arriving here gradually became tense. Originally, this battalion of soldiers took advantage of the windy, sandy night to open the pass out of fear of attracting the enemy's attention, or to avoid them using the excuse that Chinese troops had already begun to mobilize and then invading. Chinese troops mobilizing within Chinese territory, yet fearing enemy intervention – this was originally a regrettable matter, but the fact that the transferred troops were actually able to move to their destination without external obstacles was itself rare. However, on the third day after garrisoning, aircraft were discovered in the sky. The aircraft flew over the fort for about half an hour, as if it knew that troops were hidden inside. At this moment, Battalion Commander Bao Fang suddenly issued an order that brothers and civilians were not allowed to look outside the house. Soldiers are required to obey orders, so naturally no one dared to step out. But all the brothers understood in their hearts that this must be an enemy reconnaissance plane. They had long heard from senior officers that China had bought many aircraft, with foreign pilots. Moreover, to prevent enemy aircraft, each unit was allocated anti-aircraft guns or anti-aircraft machine guns. Now, not only had they not seen their own aircraft, but not even a single anti-aircraft gun had been allocated, and they could only watch the enemy's aircraft showing off its power in the sky, unable to resist. With such suspicions, a look of doubt naturally appeared on everyone's faces. An hour after the aircraft passed, Battalion Commander Bao Fang also learned of this situation and called the four company commanders to him. The four company commanders stood side by side facing him, and he stood tall, looking straight ahead, and said with a serious face: Company Commanders, do you know that my initiative brought you to garrison here? The four company commanders stood straight and did not make a sound. (340)

Research on Inkstones (6) 216

— Wuliao Ke (Bored Guest)

(4) Divisions Formed by Popularization

Since the form and carving of inkstones penetrated deeply into popular culture, they gradually spread among the provinces. Thus, within popularization, different schools emerged. When discussing inkstone making, there are three renowned schools. The works of Guangdong people have a special charm, capable of utilizing stone flaws, stone eyes, and skin to create various patterns to highlight their beauty. The works of Anhui people, such as carvings of fish, dragons, pavilions, and melons, strive for extreme detail, probably because the ink makers and inkstone makers at that time were able to study each other. The works of the people of Jiangsu and Zhejiang mostly tend towards elegance and refinement. Scholars and literati who made their own inkstones mostly loved natural charm, writing and carving themselves. Mr. Bando Kanayama of Japan most highly praises this school, and indeed it is meaningful. As for inkstone boxes, inkstone lovers also value them very much. Generally, the materials used are red sandalwood, rosewood, boxwood, and Chinese wolfberry, with the interior coated with qingguang lacquer, or pure lacquer with various carvings and decorations. The inkstone boxes made by workers in Guangzhou, Fuzhou, Anhui, Yangzhou, Suzhou, and Beijing all have different rhythms, colors, and styles, so inkstone boxes also have different schools. If there is a famous work, one can tell which school it belongs to at a glance. This kind of related and associated cultural matter is very complex, so I will not describe it in detail. I will just briefly describe some generalities so that everyone can understand.

(5) Overall Evaluation of Inkstone Material and Art

The art of inkstones reached its peak in the Qing Dynasty, and the development of the Shuikyan of Duanxi also reached its peak. Therefore, those who loved art and those who loved fine inkstone materials but did not emphasize heavy carving, even advocating natural inkstones or simply storing them as stone slabs, were divided into two factions, arguing endlessly, each with their own reasons. However, in our opinion, the main point of an inkstone is ultimately its practicality, so those who discuss inkstones must first study the material. If the material is truly good, then adding exquisite inscriptions and carvings, as well as all kinds of beautiful decorations, will only enhance its beauty. If the material is not good, but the appearance is merely decorated, it is no different from having gold and jade on the outside but decaying cotton inside, which is not desirable at all. On the other hand, if there is excellent inkstone material, but it is carelessly carved by vulgar merchants, falsely impersonating famous inscriptions, then it is no different from putting dung on a Buddha's head, as the inkstone book says, "forcefully pretending to understand, defiling this Duan friend," which is even more regrettable. Therefore, if there is good inkstone material but no exquisite inscriptions, then it is better to remain simple and uncarved. Even if it is stored as a stone slab, it is still a fine product. This is the fair opinion of the general public. The relationship between inkstones and art is generally like this. Below, I will talk about the essence of inkstones.

Pilgrimage to Europe 218

— Zhang Ruogu

(2) Nice on the Azure Coast

France is truly a paradise on earth. I will temporarily put aside the bustling urban landscape of Paris, which is second to none in the world, and first make a sketch of the natural scenery.

Geographically, France occupies a special advantage, with one coast facing the Mediterranean Sea winding around to ancient cultural lands, and the other coast along the North Sea looking out to the new world. Other countries naturally also have fascinating characteristics. For example, Italy is full of art and history, often under a permanently azure sky, shrouded in a happy climate. Switzerland is world-famous for its mountains and rivers, a great garden of humanity under the northern sky.

In southern France, there is a place called the "Azure Coast" (CÔTE D'AZUR), which is the world's famous resort for both winter and summer. It combines the advantages of both Italy and Switzerland. This is a dream world, with a spring climate all year round, a coast without winter. The lovely sun warms the soil in winter, and does not burn the skin of tourists in summer. From the beginning to the end of the year, beautiful flowers and trees are often blooming in the garden.

Important politicians, entrepreneurs, wealthy people, celebrities, actors, and tycoons from the golden countries of the New World and stars from Hollywood in various countries on the European continent all embark on journeys in winter, gathering on the "Azure Coast" to vacation and avoid the cold, chasing and frolicking under that lovely and warm sun.

The most famous place on this "Azure Coast" is Nice. The name Nice is a transliteration that has evolved from the Greek word MIKE, and its meaning is "victory." Many buildings from the ancient Roman Empire are still preserved there today. In 1860, the local population was only 26,000, but today it has surged to over 184,000, not including the tens of thousands of tourists who come every year.

In terms of natural scenery, there is a warm and lovely sun, azure skies and sea, golden beaches, the foothills of the Alps, shady olive trees, and various fragrant and exotic flowers, trees, and fruits. Nice's "Flower Market" and "Flower Festival" are world-famous. In the quieter countryside, one can see houses with walls basking in the sun everywhere, rose-colored roof tiles, surrounded by ivy or climbing morning glories. On the ochre soil, grapes, mulberries, olives, and all kinds of pine and cypress trees grow.

In terms of artificial construction, the ancient ones include churches and castles from the fifteenth century, for archaeologists to touch; modern ones include a "British Promenade" that can accommodate twenty people walking side by side, which is the largest promenade in the world. Tourists of various countries and ethnicities wander there from morning to night. Most notable are those women wearing large-brimmed straw hats and "Indian pants" with large trouser legs. They wear sleeveless, bare-chested swimsuits on their upper bodies and lead a Pekingese dog in their hands. There are also women wearing black clothes with black veils, who look like young widows from a distance. However, one can see many girls in that kind of clothing all over the street. It is said that these are the most popular women's fashions in Nice in 1933.

Nice has many歌臺舞塲, all of which are built very luxuriously. The most famous is the "Jetty Games Park" (ASINO DE JETEE), built on the sea, surrounded by the sea on all sides, entirely constructed of steel, and extremely sturdy. It has a dance hall, a theater, and a casino, much like Shanghai's Great World. In addition, there is Europe's most aristocratic hotel, the NEGREICO, and the most modern "Mediterranean Palace" (unfortunately destroyed by fire last winter), as well as the world-famous casino "Monte Carlo" (MONTE ORRLO), which is only a few hours away from Nice.

I think readers now have a fairly general impression of Nice on the "Azure Coast." Next time, I will talk about the lively celebrations of various festivals in Nice.

Free Talk

Foolish and Flattering 219

— Fang Zhizhi

Society only sees its lack of peace, and there are only more and more strange things. In the distance, there is the matter of enthusiastically welcoming a fly-by-night as a great writer, followed by Liang Zuoyou's big scene in Nanjing, followed by children marching in snow and wind to raise donations, of course for the sake of saving the country, followed by…

Those with a little conscience are amazed, saddened, and sigh at the many strange things they see. Many people's actions are like the result of too many spins, dizzy and disoriented. Examining the reasons, the first is ignorance, and the second is the desire to deliberately please. These two temperaments combine to become a kind of madness. The pitiful modern citizens, many live in this state of madness.

In fact, this has been going on for quite some time. At the end of the Ming Dynasty, someone said… "Every family has a semi-idle hall, everything is like children's play, things are mostly so-so, and the world is also carefree." Looking closely at many things now, it is almost the same situation, except that we may not "every family has a semi-idle hall" anymore.

Actions in this madness are roughly like this… First, there is a noisy commotion, making a confusing situation, such as holding a big meeting, making a commotion, and then everything remains the same. Second, many things are damaged because of this. Because of ignorance or flattery, one cannot say that they are bad-hearted. For example, a porcelain shop catches fire, and bowls, plates, bottles, and jars are smashed to pieces. In the past, many treaties were hastily and confusedly signed, out of ignorance and lack of foresight, and the Republic of China was therefore harmed. Descendants will have burdens, thinking that foreigners were therefore impressed, but not knowing that they are laughing in their hearts at our foolishness and deceiving our weakness. Third, it is no small matter. Change is easy to make people ashamed. Shamed anger, human nature, who pointed out mistakes and exposed the dark, but aroused "reverse", in the front of the executive government at that time, there were girls who bled, many people lost their lives, is caught by this madness is working and will work, should get rid of the old dark, lose the slave heart, and ask for some common sense!

On Pouring Cold Water 220

— Tao Kangde

My hometown is the same as Mr. Xu Maoyong's hometown: "When people are excitedly absorbed in something, someone, or something, someone suddenly makes a statement of enlightenment to dampen their enthusiasm" is "called 'pouring cold water'". For example, a young lady who has been married for nearly ten years and has not had a son suddenly has an enlarged belly and is excitedly absorbed in burning incense to thank the child-giving goddess, someone suddenly says to her, "Your husband hasn't been home for over a year. Your enlarged belly may be a result of the long-term humiliation from your mother-in-law for not being able to bear a son. It's better to save the money for incense and candles and ask a doctor to diagnose it." That person is the "cold water pourer". Whether this cold water is a "soft knife that kills without seeing blood" or a "head-on blow" seems to depend on whether the young lady's enlarged belly is a swelling or a pregnancy. If, unfortunately, the swelling is true, then the young lady's joy at the imminent birth will be completely swept away, and she will inevitably be discouraged, but saving the money for incense and candles to use as diagnosis money is not without practical benefit. Therefore, the right and wrong of pouring cold water depends on whether the things or people that the person being poured on is absorbed in are appropriate or not.

After Puyi ascended the throne, it is said that the old remnants from various places excitedly sent telegrams of congratulations. At this time, someone suddenly made a statement of enlightenment saying…"Puyi is just a puppet. It's better to pay homage to Puyi's photo and shout 'Long live!' than to be a subject to a puppet." This is also pouring cold water on the old remnants, but no one would dare to say that this cold water is a soft knife that kills without seeing blood, even though the old remnants may be discouraged because of it. The cold water pourer originally wanted the other party to be discouraged and to be less of a disgrace to the nation. Therefore, even if the old remnants commit suicide by drowning or hanging themselves because of discouragement, the cold water pourer does not need to feel guilty, saying, "Although I did not kill Boren, Boren died because of me." Also, for example, if there is a guy who only knows how to beat his wife at home and doesn't dare to make a sound at a strong neighbor who has slapped him ten times, suddenly sees that strong neighbor scolding another neighbor and is about to roll up his sleeves and arms to fight for justice, someone suddenly says, "You should just stay home and beat your wife." This statement is also pouring cold water, but it is not necessarily a soft knife that kills without seeing blood. Also, for example, pouring a cold cup of water on someone who doesn't measure their virtue or ability and is determined to clarify the universe, acting recklessly and making the universe a mess, can really be said to be a great deed. If he really turns back to his old business of mending vats, because of this cold water.

In short, whether pouring cold water is a soft knife that kills without seeing blood depends on who is being poured on and what they are doing. It cannot be dismissed with one stroke. Otherwise, the world will be full of things that pat buttocks, lick legs, and sail with the wind. Can the affairs of the state be done? Because now the person who pours cold water are doing this to "enthusiastic youth" so I write this essay to those like Xu Maoyong who are enthusiastic and caring about the youth.

Huaiyang Folk Song 221

— Liang

Green bamboo, knot after knot, marries a wife as black as iron, everyone says my wife is black; I say my wife is ebony-colored. Everyone tells me to divorce her; thinking it over and over, I can't bear to.

Guangzhou Correspondence 222

— Wei Li

XX:

I remember when we set off to come to Guangzhou last year, a friend came to the ship to see us off. He said to me, "Really silly, going to Guangzhou to teach!" At the time, I was a little confused, but now I know that what he said was right. I really did something stupid.

Before setting off, I also inquired about Guangzhou from friends. All they told me was that Guangzhou's weather is very hot, the cost of living is very high, and also, the Guangdong people's silver dollars are "pushed back" a bit more than our silver dollars. At the time, I thought that this little loss was nothing important, so I decided to come to Guangzhou. Who knew that when I got here, I saw that there were so many tricks! Today, I want to talk to you about the donations in Guangzhou City.

It's best to start with the salary. In our school, professors from other provinces are considered to be treated very well, with a monthly salary of four hundred silver dollars. Anyone who writes this number on paper will say that it is grand and respectable, but… but the fact is another matter. When we receive our salary every month, we have to pay 4% income donation, we have to pay 4% party headquarters fund donation, and we also have to pay 1.5 silver dollars for the volunteer army donation (said to be sent to Guanwai for the Northeast Volunteer Army to fight). These three items add up to a total of 33.5 silver dollars. I remember the first time I received my salary last year, we also subscribed to a share of the Guangdong Cooperative (?), costing 10 silver dollars. I heard that everyone who teaches has to be a shareholder, but the cooperative stock has not been sent yet. This is from the school's perspective.

You know, I came with my family. The school doesn't have a place for teachers to live with their families, so we rent a house outside. Logically speaking, rent in Guangzhou City is not too expensive, much cheaper than Nanjing—and it's easy to find a livable house. Renting a house in Guangzhou City, in addition to the rent, you also have to pay "house donation police fee". This is stipulated by the Public Security Bureau. The house donation accounts for 15% of the rent. For example, we currently pay 43 silver dollars in rent every month, so we have to pay 6.45 silver dollars in house donation, which is divided equally between the landlord and us. We ourselves have to pay 0.2 silver dollars in cleaning fees every month. In addition, there are many temporary additional donations. I'm considered lucky, having lived in Guangzhou for half a year and not having donated a single cent yet. But I saw on the donation certificate issued by the Public Security Bureau that there were many "rent donations" that had already been collected. I calculated that from 1923 to 1933, there were a total of nineteen kinds of donations. Now I'll just write a few down… "January 1923 rent loan", "1926 bandit suppression strike", "1926 Northern Expedition", "1927 strike subsidy", "1932 national salvation half-month", "1933 air defense phase one", "1933 air defense phase two", "1933 national salvation six days"… There are so many names, but unfortunately the amount of each donation is not written out, otherwise it would be a very valuable statistical material.

In Guangzhou, it's not just donating to live in a house, you also have to donate to use electric lights. Last month, my family used seventeen degrees of electricity, and the electricity bill calculated to be exactly 3.4 silver dollars. But the Guangzhou Electricity Management Committee's collector asked me to pay an extra 0.34 silver dollars. I heard that this is an additional "education fee", and I only then understood that using electric lights and running education are actually related. There is a donation for electric lights, and there must also be a donation for telegrams, because the electricity for them is the same, so why are they treated differently? I sent a telegram to Shanghai yesterday. The telegram fee calculated to be 1.2 silver dollars, but the surcharge cost 0.36 silver dollars (30%). Fortunately, there are now two airmail flights between Shanghai and Guangzhou every week, so we can also lose a little less.

These donations naturally cannot include all of Guangzhou City's donations. I'm just casually talking to you about what I've donated. You think, how much can a teacher earn every month? This donation, that donation, how can you bear to donate? Standing on the podium every day, drinking chalk dust and selling

life for others, isn't that stupid?

In fact, the loss from just donating is limited after all. The most terrible thing is the monster that sucks our blood, and its name is "unredeemed banknotes". I'll tell you about this next time.

Miscellaneous Notes on a Journey West 223

— Lu Yan

1. Before leaving Shanghai, I was wrapped and tied up again. Moving, traveling, calculating, almost every year I tie up my bedding and baggage, and several times, I've tied them up three or four times in a year.

"I'm going to tie you up, I'm going to take you to another place." I said to the bedding and baggage.

So the baggage, without resisting, allowed me to tie it up and let me take it away.

Its fate is entirely in my hands. However, what about my own fate? It is in the hands of another who does not know me.

"I'm going to tie you up, I'm going to take you to another place!" the person reaching out to me said.

So I was led away.

Every time, it's like this. It's still the same this time.

What kind of journey will the baggage go through? What kind of place will it be placed in? - It does not know.

I, too, cannot know what I will encounter, what I will see, what kind of life I will live, whether it will be joy or sorrow, whether it will be or death. Lisa is looking at me, wanting me to hug her. She doesn't know that I am her father, let alone that I am leaving. Just as I don't know what I will encounter.

Enge knows that I am leaving, but he doesn't know that I am going to a very far place. He thinks that I will come back the same day as usual. Just as Lisa doesn't know that I am leaving.

Lili knows that it will be a long time before I can come back, but she doesn't know why I am leaving. She is just like Enge, who doesn't know that I won't be back immediately.

Lan and Mother know everything. They know why I am leaving, and when I will be able to return. But they are just like me, unable to know what I will encounter, and unable to know what they themselves will encounter. (To be continued)

Spring (Continued) 224

— Zhou Lengjia

Everything is spring, everyone has spring, only my heart is cold and lonely, spring has passed from me!

Suddenly a big hand patted me on the shoulder, and a young man wearing a dark blue Western suit stood in front of me. I blankly raised my head to look at him. I recognized him. He was my friend Ping, a friend Ping who was intoxicated in a happy love dream.

"Ping, it's you." I excitedly shook his hand. I was thinking that his passionate words might warm my heart. But immediately I was disappointed. I saw his face, a melancholy face, with disillusionment and sadness in his eyes. Those dim, lackluster eyes! As soon as I saw them, I knew that an arrow of despair had shot the young man's heart. His heart was already dead.

"Ping, what are you worried about?" I couldn't help asking him. "I'm finished! She fell in love with a bureaucrat and abandoned me!" He shook his head, saying painfully, with tears in his voice.

He was walking the path I had walked in the past. This unfortunate young man also no longer had spring in his life. How should I comfort him? In front of a heartbroken person, all words of comfort are ineffective. I have this kind of experience. I can only exchange glances with him sympathetically, and accompany him on that unpleasant journey.

"What is the meaning of life!" he sighed, his voice as light and ghostly as falling flowers drifting to the surface of the water.

"Life is pain. But let us forget everything!"

"Okay! Forget everything!" he said, his eyes flashing, with a little brilliance in them. But this brilliance was short-lived, and soon disappeared.

So, we went to a restaurant, a restaurant decorated with Eastern classical flavors. Each holding the bitter cup of life, silently drinking the blood-like wine in the cup. Forgetting the era, forgetting life, forgetting love, and forgetting spring.

The sound of light clinking glasses rang out from time to time in the air, and empty wine bottles lined the table. We were both a little drunk. I staggered to my feet, poured the only half cup of wine left in my hand on the ground, and said dreamily…

"Pour a libation to this unpleasant spring!

I hope that a hopeful spring will come next year."

He smiled, and I smiled too. Our two pairs of eyes looked at each other, and both eyes contained crystal tears.

Evening (9) 225

— Jin Yi

"It's not even ten o'clock yet, and I'm already so sleepy!"

"Me too, my waist is a little sore."

"Then let's go to sleep."

So they called the maid, who made the bed for them. They changed their clothes and went to bed. The maid turned off the lights for them. They seemed eager to fall asleep and didn't say a word. Qing Song gently turned over because the moonlight was shining on her face. But she still couldn't fall asleep. She watched Qing Zhi's motionless body as she slept and heard the sound of goldfish spitting water. But no matter what, she couldn't seem to fall asleep. Her heart was always thinking about something, vague yet with a deep sense of melancholy. She closed her eyes, wishing she would never open them again, but it was still no use. She silently counted the swings of the wall clock, from one to a thousand, to two thousand; she was still so awake, even though she was anxious, there was nothing she could do.

She simply turned back over, letting the moonlight shine on her face. She opened her eyes wide and looked at the scenery bathed in the moonlight, thinking that the moonlight might wash away the depression in her chest.

The tall trees in the autumn night were rustling mournfully as they were blown by the wind, and the wall clock struck twelve again.

She let out a long, faint sigh.

"Sister, are you not asleep either?"

"Oh, I don't know why, I can't sleep!" Qing Song turned her body towards Qing Zhi again.

"I heard you turn over and thought you were asleep."

Qing Song didn't say anything more, just gazed silently in the moonlight. The cold currents of the late autumn night air made her shiver.

"Are you cold?"

"No, I don't know why I shivered."

The wall clock chimed leisurely.

"It's already one o'clock." Qing Zhi showed a little surprise.

"The long night is almost over." Qing Song said sadly.

"Sister, we must get a good night's sleep."

Qing Zhi put her arms around Qing Song's body, face to face, sleeping on one pillow, dripping onto the white sheets.

They hugged each other tightly, and in the silence, there was their light, soft sobbing. (The End)

Securities and Bond Market Thrives 229

Yesterday, the market at the Chinese Securities Exchange was still very strong. There were rumors in the market that new loans were being established. The facts still need to be confirmed. Although there were large players taking profits, large players covering short positions and new players were particularly enthusiastic. Market sentiment was high and stable. There were no signs of pullback in the near future. Interbank rates were getting lower and silver was getting looser. Shanghai's current cash reserves were particularly abundant. Bank deposit rates were low and there was an abundance of idle capital. There were many buyers with reserves to take delivery, so there was no major problem. Therefore, veteran long players were reluctant to sell, and new long players were even more eager to buy. Short players have not been able to find a way out for over a month. They even added to their positions during the last period of consolidation. Now they have actually returned their gains, covering their positions and adding to their positions. There were also those who turned from short to long, which gave the market the excellent appearance of soaring prices. New high prices were found repeatedly in each trading session. From the "18 Customs" bond to the short-term gold bond, the near-term and forward contracts for all ten bonds set new high price records. This kind of bullish trend was not subject to environmental control, but was entirely due to the abundance of strength and the supply and demand relationship of the bonds, so the bullish trend was strong and firm and not easy to stop in the short term. The course of yesterday, from morning to evening, was a very stable and slight increase in each trading session, mostly up one or two cents to three or four cents. Mediocre Conditions in the Cotton Exchange 233

The cotton market is unremarkable, lacking any brilliance. Due to the stability of American cotton and the pending review of the Bingham bill, which is partly expected to pass, there is optimism about cotton prices. However, sellers are generally concerned about the sluggish yarn market and rumors of workforce reductions. Additionally, Indian cotton market prices are weakening, and the desire to short sell persists. Currently, Japanese cotton mills are steadily developing, but according to today's news, there has not been sufficient delivery for this month.

Weak Trading in Zheng Biao Cotton

The opening of the cotton exchange saw a weak market due to poor American cotton performance, leading to strong selling pressure. Prices fell by five to twelve cents across various months. In the afternoon, far-month contracts recovered by five to ten cents. The total trading volume for the day was 359 hundred – recorded as 3,900 dan (a unit of weight). Changhe traded 2,700 dan, Yongda 1,100 dan, Xiesheng 2,000 dan, Yuantai 1,700 dan, and Shenchang 1,300 dan. Buyers included Dafu with 2,400 dan, Yuanda 1,000 dan, Shenji 3,100 dan, Xincheng 1,500 dan, Zhenda 1,400 dan, Gengfeng 1,000 dan, and Tonghe 1,000 dan. The daily high, low, and closing prices are as follows:

Bombay Cotton Industry Weekly Report 234

Last week, the market turned firm, with progress in actual positions after a bullish phase. Simultaneously, industry players were encouraged by news of Far East purchases of "White Russell" cotton. However, prices did not rise due to a lack of new stimulus. In the spot market, activity was relatively high, with considerable inquiries from Japan and interest from local factories. European transactions remained stagnant. The following is a summary of statistics for the past week (in thousands of bales):

Grain Millers Buy Back Recent Flour 235

Yesterday's flour market saw a trend of initial stability followed by rising prices in various months after the opening bell. Quotations for foreign wheat remained relatively stable, with Chicago wheat at 8/8 of a cent and Canadian wheat at 1/10 of a cent. Consequently, market activity was calm as usual after the opening. Later, as millers continued to withhold offers, and given the imminent settlement of the current month's contracts, millers, despite the lack of major transactions by outside speculators, autonomously bought back due to other considerations, leading to a positive sentiment in the near term, with the long term slightly following suit.

By the afternoon opening, the current month saw millers engaging in spread trading, buying back near-term contracts and selling long-term ones. Outside speculators were both buying and selling, with actual sales remaining limited. Based on the current situation, millers may have other intentions, such as absorbing near-term contracts to maintain standards. As a result, the current month was better by 1.75 cents compared to the previous week, April was better by 2 cents, May was better by 1.25 cents, June was better by 0.5 cents, July was up 0.75 cents, and August was better by 0.5 cents.

July Wheat Stands Out with a 4-Cent Gain 236

Yesterday's wheat market showed a slight bullish trend. Foreign wheat quotations saw minimal fluctuations, with Chicago wheat at 8/8 of a cent and Canadian wheat at 1/10 of a cent. However, market inventory was extremely limited. With the current month nearing settlement, trading volume was naturally low. The long-term outlook was subject to varied observations, leading to a generally cautious stance. June contracts, which had been offered in the morning, turned bullish, opening at 71 cents and later decreasing by 0.02 cents, ultimately closing up 0.07 cents compared to the previous week. July and August saw little trading. Ultimately, July was better by 4 cents, while there were no comparisons for the others. Based on this year's weather, industry insiders predict that future harvests will not be hopeless, so a sluggish trend should be watched for in the future. The current wheat market is smooth and prices are stable as mills are already active. Prices opened at 3.48 yuan for Bengbu wheat and 3.55 yuan for Yingzhou wheat, with a total of 3,000 bags reportedly handled by Huafeng.

Glutinous Rice Market Stagnant, Continues Slight 0.05 Yuan Decline 237

(Shanghai South) Yesterday's sources for outside speculators were mostly from the 46th and 47th districts (over 7,000 piculs), with late rice being the most abundant and nearly the 30th district showing signs of tightening. However, only Nanyang speculators were actively purchasing, with Beiyang speculators quickly ceasing activity, causing a sudden shift in the market, which turned soft. Together, the Nanyang and Beiyang speculators totaled 3,000 bags. The market for Qingjiao, Songsi, Xilian, and other goods seemed to hold steady, but the trend may decline. Although the supply of thick glutinous rice from various speculators was not abundant, sales in both urban and rural areas were particularly sluggish, resulting in a very quiet market. The market was weak, causing prices of Changbang, Sutong, Nangang, and other varieties to fall by another 0.05 yuan. The supply and demand for Duyangjian were still well-matched, remaining stable, while the change in Yuan was similar to before.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 17th and 18th district goods arrived at the port from various locations along the river. Sales on the market remained slow. However, Zhongguan white glutinous rice showed a slight improvement, with prices of high-quality white glutinous rice approaching a 0.1 yuan increase, and prices of medium-grade and lower-grade white glutinous rice were reduced by several cents. Yangdujian, Baiyuan, and Yinyuan also decreased by a small amount, while Bu Jian, Ke Jian, early rice, and thin rice saw flat and weak prices.

North-South Goods: Orchid Seeds Arrive After a Long Disruption 238

—Prices Soar—

Orchid seeds produced in Zhangzhou have long been sold out in Shanghai, and with the source cut off for a long time, there are many inquiries. The market is firm and the price has soared by more than ten yuan. Yesterday, it was heard that a batch had arrived on the Taikoo Company's Jinan wheel steamer, totaling five boxes. Samples have already been viewed, and their color is delicate and yellowish, and the asking price is 50 yuan, and it is estimated that a transaction can be made today. Since being affected by local factory cakes and Wenzhou cakes, the arrival of large soft cakes from Xiamen has also decreased. Yesterday, it was heard that the Jinan wheel steamer also transported a batch of about eleven to ten boxes, priced at about 26 or 27 yuan. As the sales in Shanghai are still active, it may be cleared.

Sugar Market: Another Batch of Zhangzhou Raw Sugar Arrives 239

Yesterday, although the sugar market saw a consistent rise in both spot and customs duties, actual sales remained sluggish. Public sentiment in the association remained difficult to boost. The asking price for 24 coarse sand white sugar was 19.75 yuan, but no sales were made. Taikoo B mark was at 20.15 yuan, No. 9 Dutch red was at 15.85 yuan, and No. 8 was at 15.7 yuan, with scattered transactions. Although the ground price of Chaozhou raw sugar was firm, the attitude of the industry was cautious as shipments had not moved in Shanghai. Yesterday, 107 bags of Zhangzhou raw sugar were transported by the Jinan wheel steamer, and it was heard that the cost still required more than 11 yuan.

Talking Points 241

—Thin Man

Nowadays, people pay attention to appearances. Clothes must be beautiful, and grooming must be neat, so that when you approach people, they won't dislike you. Even in all aspects of eating, living, socializing, and entertainment, appearances are essential. Appearance is the only key to getting along in today's world. No matter how poor your family is or how difficult your finances are, you can't ignore appearances. Even if you are short on money, you must still put on a lavish show when you go out. As the people of Suzhou say, "Soft clothes on your body, but no rice for dinner at home," that's the idea. Today's society is one that values appearance above all else. If you don't have appearances, you will be scorned everywhere. If you have appearances, even when you go to a shop to buy something, the clerks will treat you with special courtesy, and when you go to a restaurant, the waiters will bow to you a few extra times. In fact, this society is inherently snobbish.

Why is this society fundamentally snobbish? It's because it's too difficult for everyone to get enough to eat. Because it is difficult to get enough to eat, those who can get enough to eat become extraordinarily noble. By contrast, most people who cannot get enough to eat become extraordinarily inferior. In this way, differences in wealth arise in society. Furthermore, because of the differences in wealth, everyone loves to take the path of wealth and does not want to take the path of poverty, so poverty becomes the target of public criticism.

In fact, society never originally had any concept of higher or lower; these are all man-made. Because people are selfish and self-interested (naturally, this is entirely determined by objective economic conditions), society has developed hierarchies; the differences in society are nothing more than man-made relationships. For example, as mentioned earlier, people, in order to maintain appearances, cannot help but spend all their income on outward appearances, enduring hunger and cold at all costs; also, he should have bought a book to read, but because of appearance concerns, he has to take the money for buying books to buy beautiful clothes to wear. Knowledge can be neglected, but appearance must be maintained. Extending this further, workers doing work and farmers cultivating fields should always try to increase their knowledge and pay attention to technical improvements, but because of the necessities of life, they cannot spare any more thought or energy for this. Therefore, people are forced to maintain appearances due to the pressures of life, and as a result, life becomes even more difficult to secure due to appearances. So, how can people forget the "problem of life" and devote themselves to the progress of society? This requires a fundamental transformation of the objective social conditions that make "life" a "problem." Naturally, this is a big problem.

—Lie Huo

"That's it, don't trouble yourself anymore"!

At this moment, Jinmei brought me a basin of hot water to wash my face, turned around and retreated, bumped into Guan Baomei, and said...

passing on the seed! And what good is it to have a son in such a filthy world? What use is it? This is a Prisoner Seeing a General

Waste 244

—Qian Xu

A thing is naturally viewed differently from different perspectives. For example, when a writer is working, he smokes a cigarette. To himself, it certainly has great significance, because without it, it seems impossible to get "inspiration" to spring from his brain, and he uses it as a tool to excite his nerves. However, in the eyes of ordinary people—especially those who don't like smoking—it feels like a small "waste."

For example, a friend of mine was careless on a bus, and his hat was snatched by a young rascal, who sold the ten-yuan呢 hat to a middleman for two yuan. For my friend, it was certainly a loss, needless to say, and the young rascal only got two-tenths of the price, which also seems like a "waste." However, according to economic principles, this "waste" is not valid. Because although my friend suffered a loss, and the young rascal only got a very low price, the middleman gained a profit, and at the same time, another buyer got a bargain. There was no change in the hat itself.

What I want to propose in this article is waste in a broader sense.

Why has our country become so weak since the Qing Dynasty revolution, in just over twenty years? It is almost in a state of utter ruin. Everyone knows that it was caused by years of natural and man-made disasters, internal strife, and foreign aggression. In recent years, the development of capitalism and the surplus of goods in industrial countries have all used our country as a dumping ground, absorbing our cash. What is especially terrible is the large-scale import of agricultural products, which fiercely broke our "agricultural-based" camp, causing 70% of our country's farmers to become displaced. In addition, the two floods have made it impossible for them to cultivate the land. At the same time, urban industry and commerce are also teetering on the brink of collapse due to the general decline in purchasing power. Recently, in Shanghai, known as the "Paris of the East," more than 500 large stores have received "sealing" warnings. The danger in the mainland continues to increase. The number of unemployed people is increasing year by year, day by day. Under this current situation, the waste of time and manpower, if quantified with specific numbers, is an astonishing amount! Based on the current situation described above, those who qualify as bourgeoisie, seeing the bankruptcy of the countryside and the decline of industry and commerce, dare not invest in these areas and take a desperate gamble. So, the only outlet is "banks." They themselves are even more happy to spend their days at dance halls and cafes to enjoy their remaining years. And those women with some beauty have no choice but to offer their bodies, hoping to get some leftovers and maintain their daily lives.

Repeatedly tolerating and ignoring, there will inevitably be a day of total collapse, which will be uncontrollable!

However, to seek salvation, one must start from the root and quickly eliminate this terrible and huge "waste." Empty talk of "relief" is of no use.

Sister-in-law and Little Sister 246

— Ms. Jiong

According to the traditional explanation, the so-called "little sister" is what all wives call their husband's younger sister within a family.

In the past, when we lived in old families, we often saw and heard many unfortunate things arise from the mouths of the little sisters! That is to say, in a family, the happiness or unhappiness of the wife depended on the tongue of the little sister. If the wife was cunning and skillful enough to use many strategies to win the little sister's favor, then she would certainly gain some benefits. That is to say, at least, the wife would not suffer too much abuse from her parents-in-law, or be beaten and scolded by her husband. Her status would also be somewhat elevated. Therefore, from this perspective, it is so difficult for wives in the past and those still living in old families, as difficult as ascending to heaven!

I remember an old saying: "The elder sister-in-law's cunning, the little sister-in-law's strangeness." The so-called elder sister-in-law refers to the husband's older sister; the so-called little sister-in-law refers to the husband's younger sister. Both have a high position in the family. How terrifying and sinful they are to the wife! In terms of humanity, how cruel is this!

Women are already in an extremely painful and pitiful position in society! For thousands of years, they have been accustomed to the oppression of feudal customs; traditional ideas do not give them any freedom; various unequal and cruel treatments are enough to make them feel heartbroken! Who would have thought that in addition to the various social systems that strike and exploit them, there is also this unexpected, same-kind mutual killing and jealousy, the so-called little sisters. How unfortunate are those who are wives!

With the eastward spread of European trends, after the Industrial Revolution, the alarm bell of French women was broken, and they automatically stood up to demand their status and human rights in society. As a result, Chinese women also gradually responded. Since the "May Fourth Movement," they have also automatically demanded liberation and have risen up to fight against the old society in various ways. The old Chinese family system is also gradually collapsing with the torrent of the times. The little sister system has also declined as a result. This is an undeniable fact! It is also a new phenomenon that we should be grateful for. Therefore, all social phenomena are giving rise to new reflections. In addition to looking forward to the future of women with optimism, we should also work together to promote it and rapidly move it forward. Originally, in any family, let's take the old-fashioned family as an example, most couples still have passionate love for each other, but due to the oppression of that kind of bad and feudal environment, they dare not express it outwardly. Even if they love each other, they cannot show it on their faces! The little sister's harsh and painful treatment, like jealousy and cruelty, drives the parents-in-law and husband to beat and scold out of helplessness and innocence, causing discord in the family, often leading the wife to suicide and extreme pain! In the old-style family, the little sister system is simply an extremely sinful system! It acts as the fuse for family discord.

Although new families are increasingly flourishing now, all old systems are gradually being shattered and dying. In the new family, the unit is purely based on husband and wife. Pure emotions are used to supervise and help each other, so that social undertakings can develop and succeed. What a happy thing this is! However, in present-day China, the remnants of feudal thinking are still very strong. We only need to open our eyes and see, especially in rural areas, how prosperous and lingering the so-called little sister system is! Don't we see in the newspapers every day that a child bride in a certain place was beaten to death by her parents-in-law, and that a certain woman was abandoned by her husband, leading to suicide? Therefore, to say that the Chinese little sister system has completely declined is not true! In the old-style family, the cause of general discord cannot but be attributed to the trouble caused by the little sister's tongue. This is what I dare to assert, and it is a common social phenomenon.

If we pay attention now, not only in rural areas but also in cities, we often see such unfortunate phenomena. To be honest, in a society like China, everything is chaotic, a hemiplegic morbid phenomenon. The remnants of feudalism are still deeply buried in our minds. If we want to completely destroy and annihilate all old systems, we must first make an effort to thoroughly overthrow the entire system before rebuilding and compensating it!

Amateur Mailbox

Bearing Insult and Swallowing Anger 247

Editor,

I am a very young woman. I didn't continue to study after graduating from elementary school.

In 1930, when I was just over ten years old, I was married to a middle-aged man I didn't know, according to my parents' wishes. Since marriage, there has been no emotion between husband and wife, but he relies on his relatives working in politics and often bullies me. I just bear the insult and swallow my anger. Last year, because of a trivial matter, he even acted barbarously and beat me. The day after he beat me, he sent me to another place. There has been no news from him since then (the above is just a rough description of the situation).

I really don't want to endure this kind of pain anymore. I have asked his relatives to divorce him, but his relatives replied that since I have entered his family, no matter what, I will never be allowed any freedom.

I have thought about hiring a lawyer to resolve the matter or filing a lawsuit in court, but because I have no money and no relatives or friends here, how can I do it!

I can only ask you, sir, to give me a complete solution to save me from this pit of fire. I wish you good spirits!

Miao Dingzhen, late at night on the 23rd of March

Answer: The editor has repeatedly said that marriage should be based on love, and divorce is possible when love breaks down. However, in the current society, it is impossible to achieve this ideal. The reasons have been discussed in this mailbox before, under the title "Why is Divorce Difficult?" I won't go into detail here. In Miao's case, she should get a divorce in theory, but she cannot get a divorce under current law. Therefore, it seems that she can only continue to endure "this kind of pain that I really don't want to endure anymore." There is no fundamental solution. However, although there is no fundamental solution, the editor has thought of a remedy that may alleviate the pain somewhat.

We believe that the biggest reason why husbands or their families in the current society can "bully" their wives or daughters-in-law, and the wives have to "bear the insult and swallow their anger," is that the wives have to rely on their husbands to live and cannot be economically independent. If they can be economically independent, "this kind of pain" may not happen. Therefore, we believe that the best way for Ms. Miao now is to find a job as soon as possible. Don't dislike the job being small, the pay being low, or being too hard, etc. If you have a job and can be economically independent, "he" will no longer be able to "bully" you. Even if he comes to "bully" you, you don't have to "bear the insult and swallow your anger" anymore. You can fight back. If he is really unreasonable, you have money to hire a lawyer to sue him, so you won't "have no money" and cannot file a lawsuit in court.

As for what his relatives said to you, it is completely nonsense. Freedom is our right, who can restrict it! Therefore, if they don't allow you to find a job and become independent, you must not give in at all. You must resist them as much as possible and fight for the freedom to "find a job" and "be economically independent."

In short, in this day and age, you will encounter difficulties everywhere. We rarely have "perfect plans" or "smooth sailing" in doing things. Therefore, we must use the spirit of burning our boats and breaking our cauldrons to solve difficulties in everything we do. Whether you can avoid being subdued by them depends on whether you have such a spirit.
