Rain (1) 248

— Zhang Yiping

At dusk, a gust of wind suddenly swept in from the window, carrying sand and dust; it was almost unbelievable that it was the middle of March when I was still feeling hot in my lined jacket at noon. I was busy closing the window, and several sets of papers had already been blown to the center of the floor. These were originally to be returned to the students on Thursday. My temperament has never been to finish the things I have to do early, and I won't move a finger until I'm forced to, so this temperament is famous among my friends as a "lazy bug." The weather was so good today, I haven't had weather this good since winter, and instead it made me feel an inexplicable oppression. My colleagues invited me to tour the lake in the afternoon, but I didn't seem to be able to muster any enthusiasm, so I declined and slept through the afternoon alone. I still felt unwell all over when I woke up, so I wandered aimlessly around the campus. This spring in March, the flowers, trees, butterflies, and even the ponds, were all full of active vitality, but this extraordinary change in the climate didn't seem suitable for me. The peach tree in full bloom by the corner of the wall, which had just been flattering the spring breeze like a prostitute, was probably now hanging full of tears, mourning its miserable fate! Because the glass window in front of my desk was already covered with raindrops; I couldn't see the petals falling down, they had already followed the flowing water in the pond and disappeared! Spring, your momentary prosperity doesn't have the lingering desolation that winter leaves behind. Like an old man, I wandered back to my bedroom with a heart full of melancholy, as if I had lost something lovely that I couldn't remember, so I helplessly used grading papers to dispel my full of worries. This sudden gust of wind and heavy rain suddenly lowered the temperature, and I felt a little more refreshed in my heart. I changed into the cotton robe on the hanger, sat quietly, and lit a cigarette. The rain outside the window was getting heavier and heavier.

The sky was also gradually darkening, so I simply closed my eyes. Sitting alone and listening to the sound of the rain has a different kind of flavor in my heart. I didn't even notice that the cigarette was burning my fingers, and my heart seemed to melt into this quiet dusk. I don't know how long it had been, but I seemed to be drowsily hypnotized by the music-like sound of the rain. The tea servant pushed the door open and said,

"Mr. Zhu, there is a female guest."

I hesitated and turned around, trying to think within a second if there were any female guests visiting me in Hangzhou.

——Last winter, I was forced by a friend to get on the Shanghai-Hangzhou train and come here to work as an English teacher for twelve hours a week. At that time, I was recuperating in Shanghai, so although I was forced by a friend, it was also half voluntary. Changing an environment may change my mood; besides, the West Lake, with its beautiful lake and mountain scenery, is such a beautiful sanatorium! For several months, I have been happily searching for plum blossoms in the snow, exploring secluded places, and climbing to high places. All my troubles and pain have been wiped away, and I have the idea of ​​being happy here and not thinking about Shu, and growing old in this village. Although in the bright spring when red men and green women come together, I instead feel disgusted with the beautiful environment that can be agreed upon at West Lake - this may be a major reason why I often scratch my head - but after I came here - apart from my friends, I haven't notified anyone, and I don't want to tell anyone, in this instant, the female guest's slender figure had already jumped into the room in big strides. I couldn't recognize her face against the light.

Film Special

Hollywood, Where is Your Heart? Former Stars, Today's Extras 249

— Xifu

Perhaps Hollywood is heartless. That extra, wearing a groom's leather waistcoat, pulled a tall black horse, quietly waiting for Jeni Nono to ride. This was a scene in "Little Sister" (PADDY ENEXT BEST THING). The director was in charge of everything, and he didn't even know who that groom extra was. Let me tell you, he used to be a star, but now he is forced by hunger and cold and has had to condescend to work as an extra at Fox Studios. His face was full of the haggardness of the road, and his eyes were full of sadness. All kinds of misfortunes and disappointments have left indelible scars on his once cheerful face. They were scars that no makeup could cover and no lighting could hide. He was just an extra, and he deeply understood that he had to try his best to do it well, to bring out the best spirit in his small role. He got three days of work on a film, and he was already tearfully grateful to the company for helping him like this!

But only three years ago, not too long ago, he earned a salary of $2,500 a week; he was still a star of great hope. His name was Pat O'Malley (PAT O'MALLEY), and he had made "GO AND GET LT" and a dozen other sensational films. But now three days of temporary work is probably his first job in weeks, months, or even years. He earned a few dollars, maybe he can pay the grocery bill, maybe the kids are waiting to buy shoes, maybe there's no money for the bus in his pocket.

Where did O'Malley's misfortune come from? Not from drinking. Not for women. Not for nightlife. Not for lack of ability. What for? First, the stock market. Almost all of his property was wiped out. Later, he bought an oil field from a big shot, but that oil field didn't produce oil at all. So he bought a piece of barren land, and his last 30,000 dollars were also sunk in the water. All he got was a receipt for $30,000, which is still in the hands of the lawyer. Now he has an old wife and three children. His house is mortgaged for six thousand dollars, but the mortgage will soon expire, and if he doesn't make any money, the house will belong to the creditor. In the past, six thousand dollars was nothing, he didn't know how many six thousand dollars he had spent helping friends and relatives, but now... things are different... he has been abandoned by the film company and all his friends. The friends who had benefited from him in the past are now avoiding him... Sometimes he calls them, and they don't even answer the phone. The world is cold, and human relationships are fickle, causing one to sigh! I don't know how long it took, but he still braced himself and refused to show his difficulties to others. He refused to be a small actor, he wanted to find a leading role to do, but the opportunity would never grace the door of this disgraced person. He would never discuss it with the company's personnel team, because he felt that he had his record, his talent, and should never ask for pity because of his misfortune. He also knew that a person who had been a star could never be an extra again, and once he became an extra, it would be difficult to become a leading actor again. But hunger overcomes everything. O'Malley couldn't let his family's empty stomachs fight against hungry wolves. So he went to various film companies. He had no car, so he had to take the streetcar, and sometimes he had to walk to save a few cents. He also met several former stars who were also walking around various companies looking for odd jobs. He found a small job in "Little Sister". He was very grateful. He said: "I must start over again. It is very difficult to swallow my pride, but I swallowed my pride." Alas, Hollywood, where is your heart?

Audience Opinions on "Spring Dreams in the Dance Hall" 250

— Thin Man

Under the current circumstances, only this kind of film can exist, depicting some unimportant aspects of society in a light tone, with joys and sorrows, winning some people's sadness and admiration, although it also exposes some painful aspects of life in the current society, but that is just an unimportant depiction.

Speaking only within this scope, then this film cannot but be said to be quite successful. In terms of technology and photography, it has very beautiful achievements, especially the structure of the whole play is extremely ingenious and compact. For example, the manager of the dance hall, Chen Xiuwen, Cai Xiaofeng's cousin, and Zhao Yuquan, Zhang Zhi, etc., all appear once in the front of the play, and then reappear in important places, so that people do not feel abrupt, are reasonable, and quite in line with the ideal of reality. In addition, in the transitions and contacts of the plot, it can also be united by extremely economical means without feeling redundant, which is very commendable. However, there are also times when it inevitably falls into the old technique of deliberately setting up clues in the past in order to match the plot before and after, such as the breaking of the photo of Cai Xiaofeng and Li Manman, and Li Manman saying that the two words "dance girl" will bury my life, in order to respond to the fact that Cai and Li will not be able to get a complete union in the future. This is simply the echo method commonly used in sales novels, and the method is too old. I am a little dissatisfied with this point.

In terms of actor performance, everyone has average achievements. When Li Manman left Cai Xiaofeng and went back to being a dance girl, she stroked Cai Xiaofeng while at the same time having to be a dance girl for money, and the dance hall manager was waiting anxiously outside. The tragic scene was fully expressed on her face. We can see how intense her inner conflict was. This is the best section of performance in the whole play.

In short, viewed as a whole, this film has considerable achievements. But after watching it, we can't help but have a sense of emptiness, that is, the content of this film is too bland. Although it also depicts some of the sufferings of life, it is not the closest to reality, the most important, but just some unimportant depictions. It cannot give us a more enthusiastic and fresher stimulus. This is the biggest regret. However, under the current situation, only this kind of seed can exist!

For money, you have to be a dance girl, and for money, you have to be a dance girl again. Money overwhelms everything and destroys everything. The union of Cai and Li had to be sacrificed for money in the end. The material relationship in the current society is so cruelly hitting everyone. This should be the most important hint in this film. However, this hint is outside the scope.

Review of "Spring Dreams in the Dance Hall" 251

— Green Meaning

"Spring Dreams in the Dance Hall" is to depict the pain and social neglect of "dance girls." Manman in this film is a model among ordinary dance girls. Look, although she was forced by the environment to become a dance girl, she is always thinking about breaking free from these shackles and living a "human" life. After meeting Cai Xiaofeng, how does she always love him loyally - although the depiction is a bit exaggerated - but no matter how upward her heart is and how enthusiastic her love is, the treatment she receives from the environment is still very cold. She is regarded by Xiaofeng's father as an insult to the family, and she cannot escape the insults of the playboys. It is society that decides her fate, and it is society that decides the fate of ordinary weak women.

It is indeed worthy of praise that the playwright can extract this realistic theme and put it on the screen, but in the ending, when Xiaofeng brought his cousin to the prison to return her three hundred dollars, it seems that even if the playwright did not intend to distort it, he did not understand it enough. Since Manman has been given a sympathetic description in the front, then this ending is simply an insult to her. This ending is tantamount to telling us that Xiaofeng is aware (?) and has listened to his father's teachings and is united with his cousin. Here we must not forget that Xiaofeng's father is a representative of feudal traditional concepts, so the author is suspected of preaching for feudalism. The performance is a plain narration according to the development of the story, without special highlights or faults. But I always feel that it is superfluous to use a sign to imply before the tragedy happens and to use a few jokes for fun. The reason is that the former is close to superstition, and the latter destroys the plot.

Another shortcoming is that there are too many subtitles and too long dialogues. Subtitles such as "The Beginning of Cohabitation" are unnecessary.

"Rasputin" Factual Distortion

MGM Sued Story 252

— Zhuang You

Readers will remember that in the summer of last year, Shanghai tried to transport two films of the same name, "Rasputin". One was produced by MGM in the United States, starring the Barrymore sisters and brothers. One was produced in Germany, starring Conrad Veidt. However, both films were banned by the authorities in the concession. The reason was that they were afraid of causing disputes among the white Russians in Shanghai. However, the German-made film was once moved to the Shanghai Theatre in the Chinese district, while the MGM film was never seen by us.

The contents of the two films are roughly the same, and the stories are all taken from the secrets of the Russian court during the European War, depicting the life story of the demon monk Rasputin.

Now, MGM was suddenly sued in London on the 27th of last month. The plaintiff was the niece of the late former Russian Emperor, the wife of Prince Yussupov, Princess Alexandra. The reason for the lawsuit is that in the "Rasputin" film, there is a Princess Natasa, which, according to the description, is undoubtedly a shadow of herself. The film said that she was seduced and raped by La and was his mistress. The Princess believed that it was of great importance to her reputation, so she sued the London Royal Court for defamation and demanded compensation of 400,000 yuan for damage to her reputation.

The case was heard by Justice Avery. At the hearing, the plaintiff testified that the clothes worn by Princess Na in the film were exactly the same as those she wore during the European War, but she had never met La. The defendant argued. Princess Na was entirely fictional, with no hidden meaning, and the film had not been shown since it was shown last June, and the content had been deleted. There was really no reason for complaint. After two hours of debate between the two sides, the result was that MGM was found guilty of defaming others, and Princess Yussupov was awarded compensation of 25,000 yuan. Justice Avery stated that it was most despicable to slander the chastity of a woman with a happy marriage.

Wu Village's Auspicious Dream 253

The entire production work of the "Wind," directed and compiled by Wu Village of Lianhua No. 2 Factory, which is highly anticipated for public release, has been completely completed. Recently, Director Wu has been very busy, so busy that he has been neglecting sleep and food, because he has to write the instructions and make another precise cut to make the whole play coherent without a trace of slack. The night before, he wrote until dawn, and the next day at noon, he locked himself in the editing room to work. As a result, he was listless, and he dozed off for more than two hours, dreaming that he was carrying the "Wind" film to catch a train, and a gust of wind blew him into the clouds. So he rode the wind and walked, feeling like an immortal, laughing happily and waking up suddenly. Afterwards, he told his colleagues about the dream, and everyone who heard it congratulated him, because this was a very auspicious omen.

Film Novel

CATHERINE THE GREAT SCARLET EMPRESS (10) 254

— Su Mei

At this moment, the entire palace was in a state of stillness, the calm before the storm. However, alarming news was secretly spreading, and everyone was living in constant fear, anticipating the coming of a great disaster. The Empress was ill, and according to the imperial physicians, her end was near. The Grand Duke secretly smiled in his heart. The Empress, on the other hand, tossed and turned in bed day and night, cursing, "You evil gods, do you want to see me die! But I will not die, my life will be longer than yours!" Although she couldn't accept the doctors' prognosis, within the palace walls, there was already hidden fear all around... What was she afraid of? It was because in the near future, Russia would be ruled by a madman and his lover.

One day, Prime Minister Bestuzhev rushed into Catherine's bedroom and had a secret conversation with Catherine. Bestuzhev also brought a young military officer, whom Catherine did not recognize. He said, "This is Captain Volkov. When the time comes, he will lead the army in revolt. As for the government, I will take full responsibility." After a while, someone knocked on the door, and a high priest rushed in, earnestly pleading with Catherine, "The churches throughout the country implore you to adopt the Prime Minister's advice." Catherine looked at them one by one and asked, "What exactly do you want me to do?" Prime Minister Bestuzhev began by saying, "First, we need you to promise that... well... the Grand Duke, under no circumstances, can be allowed to become the tyrant of Russia." Catherine said, "Oh, so you want me to agree to have my husband put to death." She shook her head, her attitude very firm, and said, "That's not going to happen!" The Prime Minister continued, "If the Grand Duke is alive, the political strife will never end. In our long, dark Russia, even a mangy wolf knows how things will change in the future." Catherine said very solemnly, "The Grand Duke has not harmed me, how could I casually order his death?" The Prime Minister pleaded earnestly again, saying that the people of the whole country loved and supported her, and that as long as she gave the order, anything, no matter how difficult, could be accomplished. But, even at this time, when Catherine's attempts to seize power were almost complete, she was still unwilling to kill anyone—her husband, Grand Duke Peter. She said, "I have sworn to be loyal to Her Majesty the Empress and her legal heirs, how could I harm the Grand Duke!" After she finished speaking, she dismissed everyone.

Outside the door of Catherine's bedroom, she and Alexei met at the staircase. She greeted him kindly, but a sudden pain arose in her heart. She felt that she must find a way to punish this man who had deceived her. Alexei told Catherine that he had been sent abroad by the Empress and had just returned from Persia and India. She saw that he had a brand-new medal hanging on his chest, and she congratulated him, but as she was about to walk away, he stopped her. He told Catherine very sincerely, "Since I returned to the country, I have heard... now I know for sure... the Grand Duke has plans to drive you out of the palace, or perhaps... even worse, as soon as he has power in his hands!" (To be continued)
